  <div id="readme" class="Box-body readme blob js-code-block-container p-5 p-xl-6 gist-border-0">
    <article class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg" itemprop="text"><h5><a id="user-content-example-the-bankaccountstatement" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#example-the-bankaccountstatement"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Example: The BankAccountStatement</h5>
<p>The <strong>BankAccountStatement</strong> project is an example of creating a <strong>“Bank Account Statement”</strong> document. The example shows how to create a complex document that includes tables, nested tables and lists.
Also it shows how to create forms using tabulation.
Also it show the way to create two-columns page using "Left" and "Right" repeating area.</p>
<p>The example source is available in <a href="https://github.com/gehtsoft-usa/PDF.Flow/tree/master/Examples/BankAccountStatement">repo</a>.</p>
<h1><a id="user-content-prerequisites" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#prerequisites"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Prerequisites</h1>
<ol>
<li>
<p><strong>Visual Studio 2017</strong> or above is installed.
To install a community version of Visual Studio use the following link: <a href="https://visualstudio.microsoft.com/vs/community/" rel="nofollow">https://visualstudio.microsoft.com/vs/community/</a>
Please make sure that the way you are going to use Visual Studio is allowed by the community license. You may need to buy Standard or Professional Edition.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>.NET Core Framework SDK 2.1</strong> or above is installed.
To install the framework use the following link: <a href="https://dotnet.microsoft.com/download" rel="nofollow">https://dotnet.microsoft.com/download</a></p>
</li>
</ol>
<h1><a id="user-content-purpose" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#purpose"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Purpose</h1>
<p>The example shows how to create a “Bank Account Statement”, that is a complex multi-page document. See Fig. 1, Fig. 2, Fig. 3 and Fig. 4.</p>
<p>Below in brackets are the names of the blocks highlighted in the figures with brown rectangles.</p>
<p>The first or front page consists of</p>
<ul>
<li>Title with bank name;</li>
<li>Company name;</li>
<li>Questions;</li>
<li>Options;</li>
<li>Advertisement;</li>
<li>Account summary;</li>
<li>Account info.</li>
</ul>
<p>The second and following page(s) contain a table with transaction history and tables with service fees. The pages consist of</p>
<ul>
<li>Title;</li>
<li>Overdraft protection;</li>
<li>Transaction history;</li>
<li>Service fee summary;</li>
<li>Transaction fee summary.</li>
</ul>
<p>The number of following pages, including the last page, depends on an amount of data in a the transaction history. The pages are added automatically without changing the code because the data is uploaded from an external file, and the library manages the addition of  the pages.</p>
<p>The last page consists of</p>
<ul>
<li>Title;</li>
<li>Polices;</li>
<li>Instructions;</li>
<li>Balance calculation;</li>
<li>Footer.</li>
</ul>

Fig. 4</p>
<h3><a id="user-content-output-file" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#output-file"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Output file</h3>
<p>The example creates the <strong>BankAccountStatement.pdf</strong> file in the output <strong>bin/(debug|release)/netcoreapp2.1</strong> folder, unless otherwise specified on the command line.</p>
<h4><a id="user-content-1-open-the-project-in-visual-studio" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#1-open-the-project-in-visual-studio"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>1. Open the project in Visual Studio</h4>
<p>There are 2 ways to open the project:</p>
<ol>
<li>
<p>After installing Visual Studio, you just need to double click on the project file of the BankAccountStatement.csproj.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>The longer way:</p>
</li>
</ol>
<ul>
<li>Run Visual Studio</li>
<li>File -&gt; Open -&gt; Project/Solution -&gt; Choose the BankAccountStatement.csproj</li>
</ul>
<h4><a id="user-content-2-run-the-sample-application" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#2-run-the-sample-application"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>2. Run the sample application</h4>
<ul>
<li>Running from Visual Studio:</li>
</ul>
<p>Press Ctrl-F5 key.</p>
<ul>
<li>Running from the command line:</li>
</ul>
<p>In the directory with the BankAccountStatement.csproj, run the command:</p>
<pre><code>dotnet run
</code></pre>
<p>You can get optional parameters of the command line using the command:</p>
<pre><code>dotnet run -help
</code></pre>
<p>that shows specification of the command line options:</p>
<pre><code>Usage: dotnet run [fullPathToOutFile] [appToView]
Where: fullPathToOutFile - a path to the result file, 'BankAccountStatement.pdf' by default
appToView - the name of an application to view the file immediately after preparing, by default none app starts
</code></pre>
<h4><a id="user-content-3-source-code-structure" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#3-source-code-structure"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>3. Source code structure</h4>
<p>The source code consists of several files (classes).</p>
<p>The reasons to write several classes are the following (in descending order of priority):</p>
<ul>
<li>Separation of responsibility. Class Program processes command line options, possible errors during document creation and displays a report of the errors. The rest of the classes do not process the command line options and errors. They are used only to build the document.</li>
<li>Reduction of responsibility of each class. This can help to limit the size of the code for each class that improves the understanding of the code example.</li>
<li>The document consists of several pages, each class  builds its own page.</li>
</ul>
<h4><a id="user-content-4-class-program" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#4-class-program"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>4. Class Program</h4>
<p>Responsibility:</p>
<ul>
<li>Parsing command line options.
It processes the command line options using the <strong>PrepareParameters</strong> that prepares the <strong>Parameters</strong> structure.</li>
<li>Displaying prompts to user when one of the following options is presented on the command line: “?”, “-h”, “-help”, “--h”, “--help”. It is processed by the  <strong>Usage</strong>.</li>
<li>Building document.
It delegates the document building to the <strong>BankAccountStatementRunner</strong> class with the name of the resulting document file.</li>
<li>Running the application to demonstrate the resulting document if it is specified in the command line options.</li>
</ul>
<h4><a id="user-content-5-the-bankaccountstatementrunner-class" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#5-the-bankaccountstatementrunner-class"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>5. The BankAccountStatementRunner class</h4>
<p>The <strong>BankAccountStatementRunner.Run</strong> performs the responsibilities to</p>
<ul>
<li>Read the content of the file: <em>Content/sample-statement-data.json</em>;</li>
<li>Convert it to a list of objects of the <strong>Model.Statement</strong> class;</li>
<li>Read the content of the file: <em>Content/sample-statement-info-data.json</em>;</li>
<li>Convert it to an object of the <strong>Model.StatementInfo</strong> class;</li>
<li>Create an object of the <strong>BankAccountStatementBuilder</strong> class and initialize it using the converted data;</li>
<li>Build the document.
It delegates the document building to the <strong>BankAccountStatementBuilder</strong> class using the <strong>Build</strong> method.</li>
</ul>
<h4><a id="user-content-the-data-format" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-data-format"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The data format</h4>
<p>The data of the Account Statement contains in the files of Content/sample-statement-data.json and  Content/sample-statement-info-data.json.
This data are converted into the objects of the <strong>Model.Statement</strong> class and the <strong>Model.StatementInfo</strong> class respectively.</p>
<p>This data can be received from an external source, such as a database, in the real application.</p>
<h5><a id="user-content-the-sample-statement-datajson-file-and-modelstatement-class" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-sample-statement-datajson-file-and-modelstatement-class"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The <em>sample-statement-data.json</em> file and Model.Statement class</h5>
<p>This file contains a json array of all operations performed on user's account for the given period. Items of the array are json objects, each of which contains the data of one operation:</p>
<p><em>sample-statement-data.json</em>:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-json"><pre>[
  {
    <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Date<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>2020-05-26T00:00:00<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
    <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Check<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>: <span class="pl-c1">null</span>,
    <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Details<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Mobile Deposit : Ref Number :677577755404<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
    <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Deposits<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>: <span class="pl-c1">300</span>,
    <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Withdrawals<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>: <span class="pl-c1">0</span>,
    <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>EndingDailyBalance<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>: <span class="pl-c1">850</span>
  },
  <span class="pl-ii">.....</span>
  {
    <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Date<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>2020-06-24T00:00:00<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
    <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Check<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>1258<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
    <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Details<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Check<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
    <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Deposits<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>: <span class="pl-c1">0</span>,
    <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Withdrawals<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>: <span class="pl-c1">42.93</span>,
    <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>EndingDailyBalance<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>: <span class="pl-c1">2417.96</span>
  }
]
</pre></div>
<p>The <strong>BankAccountStatementRunner.Run</strong> converts this json array into the list of the objects of the <strong>Model.Statement</strong> class:</p>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-modelstatement-class" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-modelstatement-class"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The <strong>Model.Statement</strong> class:</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre><span class="pl-k">using</span> <span class="pl-en">System</span>;
<span class="pl-k">using</span> <span class="pl-en">System</span>.<span class="pl-en">Globalization</span>;

<span class="pl-k">namespace</span> <span class="pl-en">BankAccountStatement</span>.<span class="pl-en">Model</span>
{
    <span class="pl-k">public</span> <span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-en">Statement</span>
    {
        <span class="pl-k">public</span> <span class="pl-en">DateTime</span> <span class="pl-smi">Date</span> { <span class="pl-k">get</span>; <span class="pl-k">set</span>; }
        <span class="pl-k">public</span> <span class="pl-k">string</span> <span class="pl-smi">Check</span> { <span class="pl-k">get</span>; <span class="pl-k">set</span>; }
        <span class="pl-k">public</span> <span class="pl-k">string</span> <span class="pl-smi">Details</span> { <span class="pl-k">get</span>; <span class="pl-k">set</span>; }
        <span class="pl-k">public</span> <span class="pl-k">double</span> <span class="pl-smi">Deposits</span> { <span class="pl-k">get</span>; <span class="pl-k">set</span>; }
        <span class="pl-k">public</span> <span class="pl-k">double</span> <span class="pl-smi">Withdrawals</span> { <span class="pl-k">get</span>; <span class="pl-k">set</span>; }
        <span class="pl-k">public</span> <span class="pl-k">double</span> <span class="pl-smi">EndingDailyBalance</span> { <span class="pl-k">get</span>; <span class="pl-k">set</span>; }
    }
}
</pre></div>
<h5><a id="user-content-the-sample-statement-info-datajson-and-the-modelstatement-class" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-sample-statement-info-datajson-and-the-modelstatement-class"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The <em>sample-statement-info-data.json</em> and the Model.Statement class</h5>
<p>This file contains the json object. The object contains the general data of the entire bank account statement.</p>
<p><em>sample-statement-info-data.json</em>:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-json"><pre>{
  <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>BankName<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>SampleBank<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
  <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>BankNameState<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>N.A.<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
  <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>AccountNumber<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>1234567890<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
  <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>DateBegin<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>2020-05-26T00:00:00<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
  <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>DateEnd<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>2020-06-24T00:00:00<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
  <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>CompanyName<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>CompanyName<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,

<p>The <strong>BankAccountStatementRunner.Build</strong> converts the json object into the object of the <strong>Model.StatementInfo</strong> class:</p>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-modelstatementinfo-class" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-modelstatementinfo-class"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The <strong>Model.StatementInfo</strong> class:</h6>

        <span class="pl-k">public</span> <span class="pl-k">static</span> <span class="pl-k">string</span> <span class="pl-en">ToString</span>(<span class="pl-k">double</span> <span class="pl-smi">value</span>)

            <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-smi">String</span>

        }
    }
}</pre></div>
<h4><a id="user-content-6-the-bankaccountstatementbuilder-class" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#6-the-bankaccountstatementbuilder-class"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>6. The BankAccountStatementBuilder class</h4>
<p>Responsibility to</p>
<ul>
<li>Save the list of the <strong>Model.Statement</strong> objects in the <strong>statement</strong> property;</li>
<li>Save the object of the <strong>Model.StatementInfo</strong> in the <strong>statementInfo</strong> property.</li>
</ul>
<p>The <strong>Build</strong> performs the responsibilities to:</p>
<ul>
<li>Create the object of the <strong>Gehtsoft.PDFFlow.Builder.DocumentBuilder</strong> class;</li>
<li>Create the object of the <strong>BankAccountStatementFirstPageBuilder</strong> class, initialize it with <strong>statementInfo</strong> property and build the first page using the <strong>Build</strong> method;</li>
<li>Create the object of the <strong>BankAccountStatementFirstPageBuilder</strong> class, initialize it with the <strong>statementInfo</strong> property and the <strong>statement</strong> property  and build the other page(s) using the <strong>Build</strong> method;</li>
<li>Create the object of the <strong>BankAccountStatementLastPageBuilder</strong> class, initialize it with <strong>statementInfo</strong> property  and build the last page using the <strong>Build</strong> method;</li>
<li>Return the created object of the <strong>Gehtsoft.PDFFlow.Builder.DocumentBuilder</strong> class.</li>
</ul>
<h4><a id="user-content-7-the-bankaccountstatementfirstpagebuilder-class" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#7-the-bankaccountstatementfirstpagebuilder-class"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>7. The BankAccountStatementFirstPageBuilder class</h4>
<p>The <strong>BankAccountStatementFirstPageBuilder.Build method</strong> performs the responsibilities to:</p>
<ul>
<li>Create the page and set its parameters;</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>            <span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-smi">sectionBuilder</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">documentBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddSection</span>();
            <span class="pl-smi">sectionBuilder</span>
                .<span class="pl-en">SetOrientation</span>(<span class="pl-smi">Orientation</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">SetMargins</span>(<span class="pl-smi">Margins</span>);</pre></div>
<ul>
<li>Create the header with the bank name;</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>            <span class="pl-en">AddTitle</span>(<span class="pl-smi">sectionBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddHeaderToBothPages</span>(<span class="pl-c1">136</span>).<span class="pl-en">AddTable</span>(), 
                <span class="pl-c1">20f</span>, <span class="pl-c1">4</span>, <span class="pl-smi">AddMainTitleWithBankName</span>);</pre></div>
<ul>
<li>Add 2 columns with the "Company Name" and the "Question" blocks;</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>            <span class="pl-en">AddTwoPanels</span>(<span class="pl-smi">sectionBuilder</span>, <span class="pl-c1">30f</span>, <span class="pl-smi">AddCompanyName</span>, <span class="pl-smi">AddQuestionsToCell</span>);</pre></div>
<ul>
<li>Add the "Options" block;</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>            <span class="pl-en">AddOptions</span>(<span class="pl-smi">sectionBuilder</span>, <span class="pl-c1">30f</span>);</pre></div>
<ul>
<li>Add the "Advertisement" block;</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>            <span class="pl-en">AddAdvt</span>(<span class="pl-smi">sectionBuilder</span>, <span class="pl-c1">12f</span>);</pre></div>
<ul>
<li>Add 2 columns with the "Account summary" and the "Account info" blocks.</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>            <span class="pl-en">AddTwoPanels</span>(<span class="pl-smi">sectionBuilder</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0f</span>, <span class="pl-smi">AddActivitySummary</span>, <span class="pl-smi">AddAccountInfo</span>);</pre></div>
<h4><a id="user-content-the-title-display" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-title-display"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The Title display</h4>
<p>The Title on the first page (See Fig. 3) is different from the Title on the other pages.</p>
<p>It contains</p>
<ul>
<li>The Bank Name;</li>
<li>The text common to all pages: the account number, the start and end dates of the account statement, and the page numbers;</li>
<li>The bank logo common to all pages.</li>
</ul>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/159ec2c44a204237a88b7f2039ba26d7f60ce309bdd639440e05b2279014f62b/687474703a2f2f7372762d646576302e67656874736f66742e636f6d3a383038302f504446466c6f772f496d616765732f42616e6b4163636f756e7453746174656d656e7446697273745469746c652e706e67"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/159ec2c44a204237a88b7f2039ba26d7f60ce309bdd639440e05b2279014f62b/687474703a2f2f7372762d646576302e67656874736f66742e636f6d3a383038302f504446466c6f772f496d616765732f42616e6b4163636f756e7453746174656d656e7446697273745469746c652e706e67" alt="Fig. 5" title="The first page title" data-canonical-src="http://srv-dev0.gehtsoft.com:8080/PDFFlow/Images/BankAccountStatementFirstTitle.png" style="max-width:100%;"></a>
Fig. 5</p>
<p>In order to avoid a code duplication, the creating of the Title on the first and other pages is performed using methods of the <strong>BankAccountStatement</strong> class that is the base for the page building classes.</p>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-bankaccountstatementaddtitle-method" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-bankaccountstatementaddtitle-method"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The BankAccountStatement.AddTitle method</h6>
<p>The method adds the table with one row and 2 columns consisted of</p>
<ul>
<li>The Title text on the left column</li>
<li>The bank logo on the right column</li>
</ul>
<p>The method takes the following parameters:</p>
<ul>
<li>The <strong>cellBuilder</strong> - an object of the <strong>Gehtsoft.PDFFlow.Builder.TableCellBuilder</strong> class that will be used for the Title;</li>
<li>The <strong>bottomMargin</strong> - the margin values below the table, float;</li>
<li>The <strong>pageCount</strong> - the number of the document pages, int;</li>
<li>The <strong>AddTitleAction</strong> - the action to fill the left column.</li>
</ul>
<pre lang="charp"><code>        protected void AddTitle(TableBuilder tableBuilder, float bottomMargin, 
            int pageCount, Action&lt;TableCellBuilder, int&gt; AddTitleAction)
        {
            tableBuilder
                .SetBorder(Stroke.None)
                .SetWidth(PageWidth)
                .AddColumnPercentToTable("", 90).AddColumnPercentToTable("", 10)
                .SetMarginBottom(bottomMargin);
            var rowBuilder = tableBuilder.AddRow();
            AddTitleAction(rowBuilder.AddCell(), pageCount);
            AddLogo(rowBuilder.AddCell());
        }

</code></pre>
<p>The <strong>BankAccountStatementFirstPageBuilder.Build</strong> method passes the <strong>BankAccountStatement.AddTitleWithBankName</strong> method as the <strong>AddTitleAction</strong> parameter in order to add the Bank Name to the common Title (See Fig.5)</p>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-bankaccountstatementaddtitlewithbankname-method" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-bankaccountstatementaddtitlewithbankname-method"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The BankAccountStatement.AddTitleWithBankName method</h6>
<p>There must be the common text containing the account number, start and end dates of the account statement, page numbers in the Title.
The method adds the paragraph with the Bank Name and calls the <strong>BankAccountStatement.AddTextTitle</strong> method that adds the common text of the Title.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>        <span class="pl-k">protected</span> <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">AddMainTitleWithBankName</span>(<span class="pl-en">TableCellBuilder</span> <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>, 
            <span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-smi">pageCount</span>)
        {
            <span class="pl-en">AddParagraph</span>(<span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>, <span class="pl-c1">10f</span>, <span class="pl-smi">statementInfo</span>.<span class="pl-smi">BankName</span> <span class="pl-k">+</span>
                            <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> Simple Business Checking<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-smi">FNT18_3B</span>);
            <span class="pl-en">AddTextTitle</span>(<span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>, <span class="pl-smi">pageCount</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>);
        }
</pre></div>
<p>The paragraph is added using the <strong>Helper.AddParagraph</strong> method that has the parameter of the <strong>Gehtsoft.PDFFlow.Builder.TableCellBuilder</strong> class.
The static class of <strong>Helper</strong> was created to avoid a code duplication. The methods of the class will be described in the end of the article.</p>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-bankaccountstatementaddtexttitle-method" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-bankaccountstatementaddtexttitle-method"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The BankAccountStatement.AddTextTitle method</h6>
<p>In order to add the account number, the start and end dates of the account statement, and the page numbers according to the design, the method creates the table with five columns and one row.
The data location is regulated by the width of the table and the width of the columns.
Adding data to the row is delegated to the <strong>BankAccountStatement.AddStatementInfoToTitle</strong> method.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>        <span class="pl-k">protected</span> <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">AddTextTitle</span>(<span class="pl-en">TableCellBuilder</span> <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>, <span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-smi">pageCount</span>, <span class="pl-k">float</span> <span class="pl-smi">topMargin</span>)
        {
            <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddTable</span>(<span class="pl-smi">tableBuilder</span> <span class="pl-k">=&gt;</span> 
            {
                <span class="pl-smi">tableBuilder</span>
                    .<span class="pl-en">SetMarginTop</span>(<span class="pl-smi">topMargin</span>)
                    .<span class="pl-en">SetBorder</span>(<span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">None</span>)
                    .<span class="pl-en">SetWidth</span>(<span class="pl-smi">XUnit</span>.<span class="pl-en">FromPercent</span>(<span class="pl-c1">70</span>))
                    .<span class="pl-en">AddColumnPercentToTable</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-c1">23</span>)
                    .<span class="pl-en">AddColumnPercentToTable</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-c1">18</span>)
                    .<span class="pl-en">AddColumnPercentToTable</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-c1">42</span>)
                    .<span class="pl-en">AddColumnPercent</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-c1">17</span>);
                <span class="pl-en">AddStatementInfoToTitle</span>(<span class="pl-smi">tableBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddRow</span>(), <span class="pl-smi">pageCount</span>);
            });
        }</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-bankaccountstatementaddstatementinfototitle-method" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-bankaccountstatementaddstatementinfototitle-method"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The BankAccountStatement.AddStatementInfoToTitle method</h6>
<p>The method adds the account number, the start and end dates of the account statement, and the page numbers to the table's row.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>        <span class="pl-k">private</span> <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">AddStatementInfoToTitle</span>(<span class="pl-en">TableRowBuilder</span> <span class="pl-smi">tableRowBuilder</span>, <span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-smi">pageCount</span>)
        {
            <span class="pl-smi">tableRowBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddCell</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Account number:<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>).<span class="pl-en">SetFont</span>(<span class="pl-smi">FNT8_9</span>);
            <span class="pl-smi">tableRowBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddCell</span>(<span class="pl-smi">statementInfo</span>.<span class="pl-smi">AccountNumber</span> <span class="pl-k">+</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>).<span class="pl-en">SetFont</span>(<span class="pl-smi">FNT9B</span>);
            <span class="pl-smi">tableRowBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddCell</span>(<span class="pl-smi">statementInfo</span>.<span class="pl-smi">DateBegin</span>.<span class="pl-en">ToString</span>(
               <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>MMMM dd, yyyy<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-smi">DocumentLocale</span>) <span class="pl-k">+</span>
                <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> - <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">+</span>
                <span class="pl-smi">statementInfo</span>.<span class="pl-smi">DateEnd</span>.<span class="pl-en">ToString</span>(
                <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>MMMM dd, yyyy<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-smi">DocumentLocale</span>)).<span class="pl-en">SetFont</span>(<span class="pl-smi">FNT8_9</span>);
            <span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-smi">paragraphBuilder</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">tableRowBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddCell</span>().<span class="pl-en">SetFont</span>(<span class="pl-smi">FNT8_9</span>).<span class="pl-en">AddParagraph</span>();
            <span class="pl-smi">paragraphBuilder</span>
                .<span class="pl-en">AddTextToParagraph</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Page <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">AddPageNumberToParagraph</span>()
                .<span class="pl-en">AddTextToParagraph</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> of <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">+</span> <span class="pl-smi">pageCount</span>);
        }
</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-bankaccountstatementaddlogo-method" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-bankaccountstatementaddlogo-method"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The BankAccountStatement.AddLogo method</h6>
<p>The method adds the bank logo to the table's cell.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>            <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>
                .<span class="pl-en">SetHorizontalAlignment</span>(<span class="pl-smi">HorizontalAlignment</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Right</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">AddImageToCell</span>(<span class="pl-smi">Path</span>.<span class="pl-en">Combine</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>images<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>BS_Logo_2x.png<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>));
</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-addtwopanels-method" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-addtwopanels-method"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The AddTwoPanels method</h6>
<p>The <strong>BankAccountStatementFirstPageBuilder.Build</strong> uses the <strong>AddTwoPanels</strong> method to create 2 blocks of the same type. See Fig. 6 and Fig. 7.</p>
<p>To add the content of the blocks, 2 parameters are passed to the method:
the actions to fill the left and right parts of the each block.</p>
<p>The method</p>
<ul>
<li>Creates the table with the full width of the page. The table consists of 2 columns with widths 62% and 38% of the page width.</li>
<li>Adds one row to the table.</li>
<li>Creates 2 cells in the row and sets the right border for the left cell.</li>
<li>Calls the actions to fill the left and right cells.</li>
</ul>
<p>The method takes the parameters:</p>
<ul>
<li>The <strong>SectionBuilder</strong> - an object of the <strong>Gehtsoft.PDFFlow.Builder.SectionBuilder</strong> class of the section where 2 blocks are added;</li>
<li>The <strong>bottomMargin</strong> - a margin below this block;</li>
<li>The <strong>LeftPanelAction</strong> - the action to fill the left part of the block;</li>
<li>The <strong>RightPanelAction</strong> - the action to fill the right part of the block.</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>        <span class="pl-k">private</span> <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">AddTwoPanels</span> (<span class="pl-en">SectionBuilder</span> <span class="pl-smi">sectionBuilder</span>, <span class="pl-k">float</span> <span class="pl-smi">bottomMargin</span>, 
            <span class="pl-en">Action</span>&lt;<span class="pl-en">TableCellBuilder</span>&gt; <span class="pl-smi">LeftPanelAction</span>, 
            <span class="pl-en">Action</span>&lt;<span class="pl-en">TableCellBuilder</span>&gt; <span class="pl-smi">RightPanelAction</span>)
        {
            <span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-smi">tableBuilder</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">sectionBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddTable</span>();
            <span class="pl-smi">tableBuilder</span>
                .<span class="pl-en">SetBorder</span>(<span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">None</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">SetWidth</span>(<span class="pl-smi">PageWidth</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">AddColumnPercentToTable</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-c1">62</span>).<span class="pl-en">AddColumnPercentToTable</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-c1">38</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">SetMarginBottom</span>(<span class="pl-smi">bottomMargin</span>);
            <span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-smi">rowBuilder</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">tableBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddRow</span>();
            <span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">rowBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddCell</span>();
            <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>
                .<span class="pl-en">ApplyStyle</span>(<span class="pl-smi">StyleBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">New</span>()
                    .<span class="pl-en">SetBorderRight</span>(<span class="pl-c1">2f</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Solid</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Color</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Black</span>));
            <span class="pl-en">LeftPanelAction</span>(<span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>);
            <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">rowBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddCell</span>();
            <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>
                    .<span class="pl-en">SetBorderStroke</span>(<span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">None</span>)
                    .<span class="pl-en">SetPadding</span>(<span class="pl-c1">8</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>);
            <span class="pl-en">RightPanelAction</span>(<span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>);
        }
</pre></div>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/3660ebd9e46162e640f3ea3ae6d7500713c22c95728b699b32161810c125854d/687474703a2f2f7372762d646576302e67656874736f66742e636f6d3a383038302f504446466c6f772f496d616765732f42616e6b4163636f756e7453746174656d656e7446697273743250616e656c312e706e67"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/3660ebd9e46162e640f3ea3ae6d7500713c22c95728b699b32161810c125854d/687474703a2f2f7372762d646576302e67656874736f66742e636f6d3a383038302f504446466c6f772f496d616765732f42616e6b4163636f756e7453746174656d656e7446697273743250616e656c312e706e67" alt="Fig. 6" title="Two panels 1" data-canonical-src="http://srv-dev0.gehtsoft.com:8080/PDFFlow/Images/BankAccountStatementFirst2Panel1.png" style="max-width:100%;"></a>
Fig. 6</p>
<p>To create the block in Fig. 6, the  <strong>BankAccountStatementFirstPageBuilder.Build</strong> passes the following actions to the <strong>AddTwoPanels</strong>:</p>
<ul>
<li>The <strong>AddCompanyName</strong> method;</li>
<li>The <strong>AddQuestions</strong> method.</li>
</ul>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-addcompanyname-method" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-addcompanyname-method"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The AddCompanyName method</h6>
<p>The method adds the text paragraph with the Bank Name to the table cell to fill the left part of the block shown in Fig. 6</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>        <span class="pl-k">private</span> <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">AddCompanyName</span>(<span class="pl-en">TableCellBuilder</span> <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>)
        {
            <span class="pl-en">AddParagraph</span>(<span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>, <span class="pl-c1">19.2f</span>, <span class="pl-smi">statementInfo</span>.<span class="pl-smi">CompanyName</span> <span class="pl-k">+</span>
                    <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-cce">\n</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">+</span> <span class="pl-smi">statementInfo</span>.<span class="pl-smi">CompanyAddress</span>, <span class="pl-smi">FNT8_9</span>);
        }
</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-addquestions-method" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-addquestions-method"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The AddQuestions method</h6>
<p>The method to fill the right part of the block shown in Fig. 6</p>
<ul>
<li>Adds the title of "<em>Questions?</em>" using the <strong>Helper.AddParagraph</strong> method;</li>
<li>Adds the text paragraph of "<em>Available by phone 24 hours...</em>" using the <strong>Helper.AddParagraph</strong>;</li>
<li>Adds the text paragraph with the text with different fonts of "1-800-CALL-XXXXX(1-234-567-8900)";</li>
<li>Adds the table with the contact information.</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>        <span class="pl-k">private</span> <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">AddQuestions</span>(<span class="pl-en">TableCellBuilder</span> <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>)
        {
            <span class="pl-en">AddParagraph</span>(<span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Questions?<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-smi">FNT10_5B</span>, <span class="pl-c1">6f</span>);
            <span class="pl-en">AddParagraph</span>(<span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Available by phone 24 hours a day, 7 days a week:<span class="pl-cce">\n</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">+</span>
                <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Telecommunications Relay Services calls accepted<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-smi">FNT7_9</span>);
            <span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-smi">paragraphBuilder</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddParagraph</span>();
            <span class="pl-smi">paragraphBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">SetMarginBottom</span>(<span class="pl-c1">6</span>);
            <span class="pl-smi">paragraphBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddText</span>(<span class="pl-smi">statementInfo</span>.<span class="pl-smi">PhoneFree</span>).<span class="pl-en">SetFont</span>(<span class="pl-smi">FNT9_8B</span>);
            <span class="pl-smi">paragraphBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddText</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>(<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">+</span> <span class="pl-smi">statementInfo</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Phone</span> <span class="pl-k">+</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>)<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>).<span class="pl-en">SetFont</span>(<span class="pl-smi">FNT7_5</span>);
            <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddTable</span>(<span class="pl-smi">FillCallCentersTable</span>);
        }
</pre></div>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/0f00734c8ea71a1ae925f3acf1476cbd3b69358791bb8a6d7e794f1f21dd56f7/687474703a2f2f7372762d646576302e67656874736f66742e636f6d3a383038302f504446466c6f772f496d616765732f42616e6b4163636f756e7453746174656d656e7446697273743250616e656c322e706e67"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/0f00734c8ea71a1ae925f3acf1476cbd3b69358791bb8a6d7e794f1f21dd56f7/687474703a2f2f7372762d646576302e67656874736f66742e636f6d3a383038302f504446466c6f772f496d616765732f42616e6b4163636f756e7453746174656d656e7446697273743250616e656c322e706e67" alt="Fig. 7" title="Two panels 2" data-canonical-src="http://srv-dev0.gehtsoft.com:8080/PDFFlow/Images/BankAccountStatementFirst2Panel2.png" style="max-width:100%;"></a>
Fig. 7</p>
<p>To create the block shown in Fig. 7, the <strong>BankAccountStatementFirstPageBuilder.Build</strong> passes the following actions to the <strong>AddTwoPanels</strong> method:</p>
<ul>
<li>The <strong>AddActivitySummary</strong> method;</li>
<li>The <strong>AddAccountInfo</strong> method.</li>
</ul>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-addactivitysummary-method" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-addactivitysummary-method"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The AddActivitySummary method</h6>
<p>The method to fill the left part of the block shown in Fig. 7</p>
<ul>
<li>adds the nested table to the cell of the external table;</li>
<li>fills the table using the <strong>FillActivitySummaryTable</strong> method.</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>        <span class="pl-k">private</span> <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">AddActivitySummary</span>(<span class="pl-en">TableCellBuilder</span> <span class="pl-smi">outerCellBuilder</span>)
        {
            <span class="pl-smi">outerCellBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddTable</span>(<span class="pl-smi">FillActivitySummaryTable</span>);
        }</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-fillactivitysummarytable-method" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-fillactivitysummarytable-method"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The FillActivitySummaryTable method</h6>
<p>The method to fill the table by the data of the account summary</p>
<ul>
<li>Sets the table;</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>            <span class="pl-smi">tableBuilder</span>
                .<span class="pl-en">SetWidth</span>(<span class="pl-smi">XUnit</span>.<span class="pl-en">FromPercent</span>(<span class="pl-c1">80</span>))
                .<span class="pl-en">SetBorder</span>(<span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">None</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">SetAltRowStyleBackColor</span>(<span class="pl-smi">Color</span>.<span class="pl-smi">White</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">AddColumnPercentToTable</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-c1">75</span>).<span class="pl-en">AddColumnPercent</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-c1">25</span>);</pre></div>
<ul>
<li>Creates the first row with one cell in the table;</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>            <span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-smi">rowBuilder</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">tableBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddRow</span>();
            <span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">rowBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddCell</span>();
            <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>
                .<span class="pl-en">ApplyStyle</span>(
                    <span class="pl-smi">StyleBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">New</span>()
                        .<span class="pl-en">SetBorderLeftStroke</span>(<span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">None</span>)
                        .<span class="pl-en">SetBorderTop</span>(
                            <span class="pl-c1">0.5f</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Solid</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Color</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Black</span>)
                        .<span class="pl-en">SetBorderRightStroke</span>(<span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">None</span>)
                        .<span class="pl-en">SetBorderBottomStroke</span>(<span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">None</span>)
                        .<span class="pl-en">SetFont</span>(<span class="pl-smi">FNT10_5B</span>)
                )</pre></div>
<ul>
<li>Expands the cell to 2 columns;</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>                .<span class="pl-en">SetColSpan</span>(<span class="pl-c1">2</span>)</pre></div>
<ul>
<li>Fills the cell by the title text;</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>                .<span class="pl-en">AddParagraphToCell</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Activity summary<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);</pre></div>
<ul>
<li>Fills the rows of the table using the <strong>FillActivitySummaryTableRow</strong> method by passing the <strong>Field</strong> array with the data of the account summary to the table.</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>            <span class="pl-en">FillActivitySummaryTableRow</span>(<span class="pl-smi">tableBuilder</span>, <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-en">Field</span>[] {
                        <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-en">Field</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Beginning balance on <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">+</span>
                            <span class="pl-smi">statementInfo</span>.<span class="pl-smi">DateBegin</span>.<span class="pl-en">ToString</span>(
                                <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>MMMM dd, yyyy<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-smi">DocumentLocale</span>),
                            <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>$<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">+</span> <span class="pl-smi">StatementInfo</span>.<span class="pl-en">ToString</span>(<span class="pl-smi">statementInfo</span>.<span class="pl-smi">BeginningBalance</span>)),
                        <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-en">Field</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Deposits/Credits<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
                            <span class="pl-smi">StatementInfo</span>.<span class="pl-en">ToString</span>(<span class="pl-smi">statementInfo</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Deposits</span>)),
                        <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-en">Field</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Withdrawals/Debits<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
                            <span class="pl-smi">StatementInfo</span>.<span class="pl-en">ToString</span>(<span class="pl-smi">statementInfo</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Withdrawals</span>)),
                        <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-en">Field</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Ending balance on <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">+</span>
                            <span class="pl-smi">statementInfo</span>.<span class="pl-smi">DateEnd</span>.<span class="pl-en">ToString</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>MMMM dd, yyyy<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
                            <span class="pl-smi">DocumentLocale</span>),
                            <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>$<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">+</span> <span class="pl-smi">StatementInfo</span>.<span class="pl-en">ToString</span>(<span class="pl-smi">statementInfo</span>.<span class="pl-smi">EndingBalance</span>)),
                        <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-en">Field</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Average ledger balance this period<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
                            <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>$<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">+</span> <span class="pl-smi">StatementInfo</span>.<span class="pl-en">ToString</span>(<span class="pl-smi">statementInfo</span>.<span class="pl-smi">AverageBalance</span>))
                    });
</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-fillactivitysummarytablerow-method" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-fillactivitysummarytablerow-method"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The FillActivitySummaryTableRow method</h6>
<p>The method adds the rows to the table and fills them using the <strong>Field</strong> array with the data of the account summary.</p>
<p>The rows' cells have 4 different styles (See Fig. 7):</p>
<ul>
<li>The text of the 4th row must have the Bold font;</li>
<li>The right cell must have the Right align.</li>
</ul>
<p>The large margin must be above the last row.</p>
<p>Therefore, the method first defines 4 styles. Then, the method adds the rows applying the style and using the <strong>TableCellBuilder.SetPadding</strong> for the last line in the <strong>for</strong> cycle through the array.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>        <span class="pl-k">private</span> <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">FillActivitySummaryTableRow</span>(<span class="pl-en">TableBuilder</span> <span class="pl-smi">tableBuilder</span>, <span class="pl-en">Field</span>[] <span class="pl-smi">fields</span>)
        {
            <span class="pl-en">StyleBuilder</span> <span class="pl-smi">style1l</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">StyleBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">New</span>().<span class="pl-en">SetBorderStroke</span>(<span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">None</span>);
            <span class="pl-en">StyleBuilder</span> <span class="pl-smi">style1r</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">StyleBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">New</span>().<span class="pl-en">SetBorderStroke</span>(<span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">None</span>);
            <span class="pl-en">StyleBuilder</span> <span class="pl-smi">style2l</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">StyleBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">New</span>()
                .<span class="pl-en">SetBorderRightStroke</span>(<span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">None</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">SetBorderTop</span>(<span class="pl-c1">2f</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Solid</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Color</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Black</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">SetBorderLeftStroke</span>(<span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">None</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">SetBorderBottomStroke</span>(<span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">None</span>);
            <span class="pl-en">StyleBuilder</span> <span class="pl-smi">style2r</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">StyleBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">New</span>()
                .<span class="pl-en">SetBorderRightStroke</span>(<span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">None</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">SetBorderTop</span>(<span class="pl-c1">2f</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Solid</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Color</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Black</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">SetBorderLeftStroke</span>(<span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">None</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">SetBorderBottomStroke</span>(<span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">None</span>);
            <span class="pl-k">for</span> (<span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-smi">i</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-smi">l</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">fields</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Length</span>; <span class="pl-smi">i</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span> <span class="pl-smi">l</span>; <span class="pl-smi">i</span><span class="pl-k">++</span>)
            {
                <span class="pl-en">StyleBuilder</span> <span class="pl-smi">stylel</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">i</span> <span class="pl-k">!=</span> <span class="pl-c1">3</span> <span class="pl-k">?</span> <span class="pl-smi">style1l</span> <span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-smi">style2l</span>;
                <span class="pl-en">StyleBuilder</span> <span class="pl-smi">styler</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">i</span> <span class="pl-k">!=</span> <span class="pl-c1">3</span> <span class="pl-k">?</span> <span class="pl-smi">style1r</span> <span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-smi">style2r</span>;
                <span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-smi">font</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">i</span> <span class="pl-k">!=</span> <span class="pl-c1">3</span> <span class="pl-k">?</span> <span class="pl-smi">FNT7_2</span> <span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-smi">FNT7_2B</span>;
                <span class="pl-en">Field</span> <span class="pl-smi">field</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">fields</span>[<span class="pl-smi">i</span>];
                <span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-smi">rowBuilder</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">tableBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddRow</span>();
                <span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">rowBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddCell</span>();
                <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>
                    .<span class="pl-en">ApplyStyle</span>(<span class="pl-smi">stylel</span>)
                    .<span class="pl-en">SetFont</span>(<span class="pl-smi">font</span>);
                <span class="pl-k">if</span> (<span class="pl-smi">i</span> <span class="pl-k">==</span> <span class="pl-smi">l</span> <span class="pl-k">-</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span>)
                {
                    <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">SetPadding</span>(<span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">15</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>);
                }
                <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>
                    .<span class="pl-en">AddParagraph</span>(<span class="pl-smi">field</span>.<span class="pl-smi">name</span>);
                <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">rowBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddCell</span>();
                <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>
                    .<span class="pl-en">ApplyStyle</span>(<span class="pl-smi">styler</span>)
                    .<span class="pl-en">SetFont</span>(<span class="pl-smi">font</span>)
                    .<span class="pl-en">SetHorizontalAlignment</span>(<span class="pl-smi">HorizontalAlignment</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Right</span>);
                <span class="pl-k">if</span> (<span class="pl-smi">i</span> <span class="pl-k">==</span> <span class="pl-smi">l</span> <span class="pl-k">-</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span>)
                {
                    <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">SetPadding</span>(<span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">16</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>);
                }
                <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>
                    .<span class="pl-en">AddParagraph</span>(<span class="pl-smi">field</span>.<span class="pl-smi">value</span>);
            }
        }
</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-addaccountinfo-method" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-addaccountinfo-method"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The AddAccountInfo method</h6>
<p>The right part of the block consists of 7 paragraphs with different styles (See Fig. 7). The method adds them using the <strong>Helper.AddParagraph</strong> method that takes the parameter of the <strong>Gehtsoft.PDFFlow.Builder.TableCellBuilder</strong> class.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>        <span class="pl-k">private</span> <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">AddAccountInfo</span>(<span class="pl-en">TableCellBuilder</span> <span class="pl-smi">outerCellBuilder</span>)
        {
            <span class="pl-en">AddParagraph</span>(<span class="pl-smi">outerCellBuilder</span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Account number:<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-smi">FNT7_2</span>, <span class="pl-c1">6</span>);
            <span class="pl-en">AddParagraph</span>(<span class="pl-smi">outerCellBuilder</span>, <span class="pl-smi">statementInfo</span>.<span class="pl-smi">CompanyName</span>, <span class="pl-smi">FNT7_2B</span>);
            <span class="pl-en">AddParagraph</span>(<span class="pl-smi">outerCellBuilder</span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>New York account terms and conditions apply<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, 
                <span class="pl-smi">FNT7</span>, <span class="pl-c1">6</span>);
            <span class="pl-en">AddParagraph</span>(<span class="pl-smi">outerCellBuilder</span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>For Direct Deposit use<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-smi">FNT7_2</span>);
            <span class="pl-en">AddParagraph</span>(<span class="pl-smi">outerCellBuilder</span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Routing Number (RTN): <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">+</span>
                            <span class="pl-smi">statementInfo</span>.<span class="pl-smi">DepositRTN</span>, <span class="pl-smi">FNT7</span>, <span class="pl-c1">6</span>);
            <span class="pl-en">AddParagraph</span>(<span class="pl-smi">outerCellBuilder</span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>For Wire Transfers use<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-smi">FNT7_2</span>);
            <span class="pl-en">AddParagraph</span>(<span class="pl-smi">outerCellBuilder</span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Routing Number(RTN): <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">+</span> 
                            <span class="pl-smi">statementInfo</span>.<span class="pl-smi">WireRTN</span>, <span class="pl-smi">FNT7_2</span>);
        }
</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-addoptions-method" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-addoptions-method"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The AddOptions method</h6>
<p>The method creates the <strong>Options</strong> block. See Fig. 8</p>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/e7301b1815d33cb26fb133a55966480d13e13ec24595bf2d1e23269c0847e7e7/687474703a2f2f7372762d646576302e67656874736f66742e636f6d3a383038302f504446466c6f772f496d616765732f42616e6b4163636f756e7453746174656d656e7446697273744f7074696f6e732e706e67"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/e7301b1815d33cb26fb133a55966480d13e13ec24595bf2d1e23269c0847e7e7/687474703a2f2f7372762d646576302e67656874736f66742e636f6d3a383038302f504446466c6f772f496d616765732f42616e6b4163636f756e7453746174656d656e7446697273744f7074696f6e732e706e67" alt="Fig. 8" title="Options" data-canonical-src="http://srv-dev0.gehtsoft.com:8080/PDFFlow/Images/BankAccountStatementFirstOptions.png" style="max-width:100%;"></a>
Fig. 8</p>
<p>The column is the table with 2 columns with</p>
<ul>
<li>The "<em>Your Business and SampleBank</em>" text in the left column;</li>
<li>The account options in the right column.</li>
</ul>
<p>The method</p>
<ul>
<li>Creates the table with the full width of the page. The table consists of one row and 2 columns with widths 63% and 37% of the page width.</li>
<li>Adds 2 cells to the row.</li>
<li>Sets the top borders for the cells to display lines above them. In order to add a gap between the lines on the top, the method sets the left border for the right cell. The left border is set up with 10 pt. width and white color. The color is not visible and separates the borders between the cells.</li>
</ul>
<p>The cells are filled using the <strong>AddYourBusiness</strong> and <strong>AddOptionsToCell</strong> methods.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>        <span class="pl-k">private</span> <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">AddOptions</span>(<span class="pl-en">SectionBuilder</span> <span class="pl-smi">sectionBuilder</span>, <span class="pl-k">float</span> <span class="pl-smi">bottomMargin</span>)
        {
            <span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-smi">tableBuilder</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">sectionBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddTable</span>();
            <span class="pl-smi">tableBuilder</span>
                .<span class="pl-en">SetBorder</span>(<span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">None</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">SetWidth</span>(<span class="pl-smi">PageWidth</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">AddColumnPercentToTable</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-c1">63</span>).<span class="pl-en">AddColumnPercentToTable</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-c1">37</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">SetMarginBottom</span>(<span class="pl-smi">bottomMargin</span>);
            <span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-smi">rowBuilder</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">tableBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddRow</span>();
            <span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">rowBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddCell</span>();
            <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>
                .<span class="pl-en">ApplyStyle</span>(<span class="pl-smi">StyleBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">New</span>()
                    .<span class="pl-en">SetBorderTop</span>(<span class="pl-c1">2f</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Solid</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Color</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Black</span>));
            <span class="pl-en">AddYourBusiness</span>(<span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>);
            <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">rowBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddCell</span>();
            <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>
                .<span class="pl-en">ApplyStyle</span>(<span class="pl-smi">StyleBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">New</span>()
                    .<span class="pl-en">SetBorderLeft</span>(<span class="pl-c1">10f</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Solid</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Color</span>.<span class="pl-smi">White</span>)
                    .<span class="pl-en">SetBorderTop</span>(<span class="pl-c1">2f</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Solid</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Color</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Black</span>))
                .<span class="pl-en">SetPadding</span>(<span class="pl-c1">8</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>);
            <span class="pl-en">AddOptionsToCell</span>(<span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>);
        }
</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-addyourbusiness-method" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-addyourbusiness-method"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The AddYourBusiness method</h6>
<p>The method fills the left part of the block shown in Fig. 8 by the text.
The method adds the paragraph with the "<em>Your Business and SampleBank</em>" text using the <strong>Helper.AddParagraph</strong> method.
The method sets the next paragraph since the paragraph has the URL added using the <strong>ParagraphBuilder.SetUrlStyle</strong> and <strong>ParagraphBuilder.AddUrlToParagraph</strong>.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>        <span class="pl-k">private</span> <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">AddYourBusiness</span>(<span class="pl-en">TableCellBuilder</span> <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>)
        {
            <span class="pl-en">AddParagraph</span>(<span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Your Business and <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
