                            <span class="pl-k">+</span> <span class="pl-smi">statementInfo</span>.<span class="pl-smi">BankName</span>, <span class="pl-smi">FNT13B</span>);
            <span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-smi">paragraphBuilder</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddParagraph</span>();
            <span class="pl-smi">paragraphBuilder</span>
                .<span class="pl-en">SetUrlStyle</span>(
                    <span class="pl-smi">StyleBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">New</span>()
                        .<span class="pl-en">SetFontColor</span>(<span class="pl-smi">Color</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Blue</span>)
                        .<span class="pl-en">SetFontName</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Helvetica<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>)
                        .<span class="pl-en">SetFontSize</span>(<span class="pl-c1">7.5f</span>)
                        .<span class="pl-en">SetFontUnderline</span>(<span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Solid</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Color</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Blue</span>)
                        .<span class="pl-en">SetBorder</span>(<span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">None</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Color</span>.<span class="pl-smi">White</span>)
                    )
                .<span class="pl-en">SetFont</span>(<span class="pl-smi">FNT7_5</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">AddTextToParagraph</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>The plans you establish today will shape your business far into the future. The heart of the planning process is your business plan. Take the time now to build a strong foundation.<span class="pl-cce">\n</span>Find out more at <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">AddUrlToParagraph</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>https://<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">+</span> <span class="pl-smi">statementInfo</span>.<span class="pl-smi">BusinessPlan</span>, 
                    <span class="pl-smi">statementInfo</span>.<span class="pl-smi">BusinessPlan</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">AddTextToParagraph</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>.<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);
        }
</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-addoptionstocell-method" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-addoptionstocell-method"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The AddOptionsToCell method</h6>
<p>The method fills the right part of the block shown in Fig. 8 by the text and the checkboxes.
The method adds the paragraph with the "<em>Account options</em>" text using the <strong>Helper.AddParagraph</strong> method.
The method sets the next paragraph since the paragraph has the URL added using the <strong>ParagraphBuilder.SetUrlStyle</strong> and <strong>ParagraphBuilder.AddUrlToParagraph</strong>.
The checkboxes are added using the <strong>AddCheckBoxes</strong> method with the <strong>Field</strong> array.  One <strong>Field</strong> is for one checkbox.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>        <span class="pl-k">private</span> <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">AddOptionsToCell</span>(<span class="pl-en">TableCellBuilder</span> <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>)
        {
            <span class="pl-en">AddParagraph</span>(<span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Account options<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-smi">FNT10_5B</span>);
            <span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-smi">paragraphBuilder</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddParagraph</span>();
            <span class="pl-smi">paragraphBuilder</span>
                .<span class="pl-en">SetUrlStyle</span>(
                    <span class="pl-smi">StyleBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">New</span>()
                        .<span class="pl-en">SetFontColor</span>(<span class="pl-smi">Color</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Blue</span>)
                        .<span class="pl-en">SetFontName</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Helvetica<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>)
                        .<span class="pl-en">SetFontSize</span>(<span class="pl-c1">7f</span>)
                        .<span class="pl-en">SetFontUnderline</span>(<span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Solid</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Color</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Blue</span>)
                    )
                .<span class="pl-en">SetFont</span>(<span class="pl-smi">FNT7</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">AddTextToParagraph</span>(
                    <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>A check mark in the box indicates you have these convenient services with your account(s). Go to <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">AddUrlToParagraph</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>https://<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">+</span> 
                <span class="pl-smi">statementInfo</span>.<span class="pl-smi">AccountOptions</span>, <span class="pl-smi">statementInfo</span>.<span class="pl-smi">AccountOptions</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">AddTextToParagraph</span>(
                    <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> or call the number above if you have questions or if you would like to add new services<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);
            <span class="pl-en">Field</span>[] <span class="pl-smi">fields</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-en">Field</span>[]
            {
                <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-en">Field</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Business Online Banking<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>true<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>),
                <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-en">Field</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Online Statements<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>true<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>),
                <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-en">Field</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Business Bill Pay<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>true<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>),
                <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-en">Field</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Business Spending Report<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>true<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>),
                <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-en">Field</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Overdraft Protection<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>true<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>),
            };
            <span class="pl-en">AddCheckBoxes</span>(<span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>, <span class="pl-smi">fields</span>);
        }
</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-addcheckboxes-method" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-addcheckboxes-method"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The AddCheckBoxes method</h6>
<p>The method adds the checkboxes to the table's cell.
To align the checkboxes to the right of the cell, the method adds the nested table to the cell.
The method creates columns 60% width for the label and 40% width for the checkbox in the table.
The method adds one row for each checkbox, adds the label rows and the checkbox symbols to the cells in the <strong>foreach</strong> cycle.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>        <span class="pl-k">private</span> <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">AddCheckBoxes</span>(<span class="pl-en">TableCellBuilder</span> <span class="pl-smi">outerCellBuilder</span>, <span class="pl-en">Field</span>[] <span class="pl-smi">fields</span>)
        {
            <span class="pl-smi">outerCellBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddTable</span>(<span class="pl-smi">tableBuilder</span> <span class="pl-k">=&gt;</span> 
            {
                <span class="pl-smi">tableBuilder</span>
                    .<span class="pl-en">SetBorder</span>(<span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">None</span>)
                    .<span class="pl-en">SetWidth</span>(<span class="pl-smi">XUnit</span>.<span class="pl-en">FromPercent</span>(<span class="pl-c1">100</span>))
                    .<span class="pl-en">SetMarginTop</span>(<span class="pl-c1">10</span>)
                    .<span class="pl-en">AddColumnPercentToTable</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-c1">60</span>).<span class="pl-en">AddColumnPercent</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-c1">40</span>);
                <span class="pl-k">foreach</span>(<span class="pl-en">Field</span> <span class="pl-smi">field</span> <span class="pl-k">in</span> <span class="pl-smi">fields</span>)
                {
                    <span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-smi">tableRowBuilder</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">tableBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddRow</span>();
                    <span class="pl-smi">tableRowBuilder</span>
                        .<span class="pl-en">SetBorderStroke</span>(<span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">None</span>);
                    <span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">tableRowBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddCell</span>();
                    <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">SetFont</span>(<span class="pl-smi">FNT7_2</span>).<span class="pl-en">AddParagraph</span>(<span class="pl-smi">field</span>.<span class="pl-smi">name</span>);
                    <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">tableRowBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddCell</span>();
                    <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">SetHorizontalAlignment</span>(<span class="pl-smi">HorizontalAlignment</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Right</span>);
                    <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">SetFont</span>(<span class="pl-smi">FNTZ8</span>).<span class="pl-en">AddParagraphToCell</span>(<span class="pl-smi">CHECK_BOX</span>);
                }
            });
        }
</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-addadvt-method" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-addadvt-method"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The AddAdvt method</h6>
<p>The method creates the <strong>Advertisement</strong> block. See Fig. 9.</p>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/8955479f88efedd47a18ed7e016dafdb926ceaa239092da6ba4da110bd356f38/687474703a2f2f7372762d646576302e67656874736f66742e636f6d3a383038302f504446466c6f772f496d616765732f42616e6b4163636f756e7453746174656d656e744669727374416476742e706e67"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/8955479f88efedd47a18ed7e016dafdb926ceaa239092da6ba4da110bd356f38/687474703a2f2f7372762d646576302e67656874736f66742e636f6d3a383038302f504446466c6f772f496d616765732f42616e6b4163636f756e7453746174656d656e744669727374416476742e706e67" alt="Fig. 9" title="Advertisement" data-canonical-src="http://srv-dev0.gehtsoft.com:8080/PDFFlow/Images/BankAccountStatementFirstAdvt.png" style="max-width:100%;"></a>
Fig. 9</p>
<p>The method adds the line separating this block from the previous block. The method adds the paragraph with the advertisement text using the <strong>Helper.AddParagraph</strong>.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>        <span class="pl-k">private</span> <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">AddAdvt</span>(<span class="pl-en">SectionBuilder</span> <span class="pl-smi">sectionBuilder</span>, <span class="pl-k">float</span> <span class="pl-smi">bottomMargin</span>)
        {
            <span class="pl-smi">sectionBuilder</span>
                .<span class="pl-en">AddLine</span>(<span class="pl-smi">PageWidth</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0.5f</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Solid</span>).<span class="pl-en">SetMarginBottom</span>(<span class="pl-c1">12</span>);
            <span class="pl-en">AddParagraph</span>(<span class="pl-smi">sectionBuilder</span>, <span class="pl-smi">statementInfo</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Advt</span>, <span class="pl-smi">FNT7_5</span>, <span class="pl-smi">bottomMargin</span>);
        }
</pre></div>
<h4><a id="user-content-8-the-bankaccountstatementsecondpagebuilder-class" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#8-the-bankaccountstatementsecondpagebuilder-class"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>8. The BankAccountStatementSecondPageBuilder class</h4>
<p>The <strong>BankAccountStatementSecondPageBuilder.Build</strong> method performs responsibilities to :</p>
<ul>
<li>Create the page and set its parameters;</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>            <span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-smi">sectionBuilder</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">documentBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddSection</span>();
            <span class="pl-smi">sectionBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">SetOrientation</span>(<span class="pl-smi">Orientation</span>).<span class="pl-en">SetMargins</span>(<span class="pl-smi">Margins</span>);</pre></div>
<ul>
<li>Create the header without the bank name;</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>            <span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-smi">headerBuilder</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">sectionBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddHeaderToBothPages</span>(<span class="pl-c1">80</span>);
            <span class="pl-en">AddTitle</span>(<span class="pl-smi">headerBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddTable</span>()
                , <span class="pl-c1">20f</span>, <span class="pl-c1">4</span>, <span class="pl-smi">AddCommonPageTitle</span>);</pre></div>
<ul>
<li>Add the line separating the header from the rest of the page content;</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>            <span class="pl-smi">headerBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddLine</span>(<span class="pl-smi">PageWidth</span>, <span class="pl-c1">2f</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Solid</span>);</pre></div>
<ul>
<li>Add the blocks of "Overdraft protection", "Transaction history", "Service fee summary", "Transaction fee summary".</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>            <span class="pl-en">AddOverdraftProtection</span>(<span class="pl-smi">sectionBuilder</span>, <span class="pl-c1">32f</span>);
            <span class="pl-en">AddTransactionHistory</span>(<span class="pl-smi">sectionBuilder</span>, <span class="pl-c1">12f</span>);
            <span class="pl-en">AddServiceFeeSummary</span>(<span class="pl-smi">sectionBuilder</span>);
            <span class="pl-en">AddTransactionFeeSummary</span>(<span class="pl-smi">sectionBuilder</span>);</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-title-display-1" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-title-display-1"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The Title display</h6>
<p>All <em>Titles</em> from the second page (See Fig. 10) contain</p>
<ul>
<li>The <em>Title</em> text common to all pages: the account number, the start and end dates of the account statement, and the page numbers;</li>
<li>The bank logo common to all pages.</li>
</ul>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/068ea815cd8957545c6f91ebfe15cede8fdcb319899abc16b8b63006105f9ce4/687474703a2f2f7372762d646576302e67656874736f66742e636f6d3a383038302f504446466c6f772f496d616765732f42616e6b4163636f756e7453746174656d656e744e6578745469746c652e706e67"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/068ea815cd8957545c6f91ebfe15cede8fdcb319899abc16b8b63006105f9ce4/687474703a2f2f7372762d646576302e67656874736f66742e636f6d3a383038302f504446466c6f772f496d616765732f42616e6b4163636f756e7453746174656d656e744e6578745469746c652e706e67" alt="Fig. 10" title="The next page title" data-canonical-src="http://srv-dev0.gehtsoft.com:8080/PDFFlow/Images/BankAccountStatementNextTitle.png" style="max-width:100%;"></a>
Fig. 10</p>
<p>The separate parts of the Title are created using the method of the <strong>BankAccountStatement.AddTitle</strong> base class.</p>
<p>The <strong>BankAccountStatementSecondPageBuilder.Build</strong> method passes the <strong>BankAccountStatement.AddCommonPageTitle</strong> method as the <strong>AddTitleAction</strong> parameter in order to add the common <em>Title</em>.</p>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-bankaccountstatementaddcommonpagetitle-method" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-bankaccountstatementaddcommonpagetitle-method"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The BankAccountStatement.AddCommonPageTitle method</h6>
<p>It calls the <strong>BankAccountStatement.AddTextTitle</strong> method to add the common text to the <em>Title</em> with the 10 pt. top margin.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>        <span class="pl-k">protected</span> <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">AddCommonPageTitle</span>(<span class="pl-en">TableCellBuilder</span> <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>, <span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-smi">pageCount</span>)
        {
            <span class="pl-en">AddTextTitle</span>(<span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>, <span class="pl-smi">pageCount</span>, <span class="pl-c1">10</span>);
        }
</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-addoverdraftprotection-method" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-addoverdraftprotection-method"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The AddOverdraftProtection method</h6>
<p>The method adds the "<strong>Overdraft Protection</strong>" block shown in Fig. 11.</p>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/ded21d1902c2593fbcb6d1710c2fc260c015fa94e68df530d13ae7dd2d97fcd8/687474703a2f2f7372762d646576302e67656874736f66742e636f6d3a383038302f504446466c6f772f496d616765732f42616e6b4163636f756e7453746174656d656e744e6578744f766572647261667450726f74656374696f6e2e706e67"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/ded21d1902c2593fbcb6d1710c2fc260c015fa94e68df530d13ae7dd2d97fcd8/687474703a2f2f7372762d646576302e67656874736f66742e636f6d3a383038302f504446466c6f772f496d616765732f42616e6b4163636f756e7453746174656d656e744e6578744f766572647261667450726f74656374696f6e2e706e67" alt="Fig. 11" title="Overdraft Protection" data-canonical-src="http://srv-dev0.gehtsoft.com:8080/PDFFlow/Images/BankAccountStatementNextOverdraftProtection.png" style="max-width:100%;"></a>
Fig. 11</p>
<p>The paragraph is added using the <strong>Helper.AddParagraph</strong> method that takes the object of the <strong>Gehtsoft.PDFFlow.Builder.SectionBuilder</strong> class as the parameter.</p>
<p>The method adds</p>
<ul>
<li>The paragraph with the "<em>Overdraft Protection</em>" text;</li>
<li>The paragraph with the "<em>Your account is linked to...</em>" text.</li>
</ul>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-addtransactionhistory-method" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-addtransactionhistory-method"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The AddTransactionHistory method</h6>
<p>The method adds the "<strong>Transaction history</strong>" block shown in Fig. 12.</p>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/b77971ca67f6a42febb85153db5c94ca84765e7b43c03873d9f8ac45a56eb94b/687474703a2f2f7372762d646576302e67656874736f66742e636f6d3a383038302f504446466c6f772f496d616765732f42616e6b4163636f756e7453746174656d656e744e6578745472616e73616374696f6e686973746f72792e706e67"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/b77971ca67f6a42febb85153db5c94ca84765e7b43c03873d9f8ac45a56eb94b/687474703a2f2f7372762d646576302e67656874736f66742e636f6d3a383038302f504446466c6f772f496d616765732f42616e6b4163636f756e7453746174656d656e744e6578745472616e73616374696f6e686973746f72792e706e67" alt="Fig. 12" title="Transaction history" data-canonical-src="http://srv-dev0.gehtsoft.com:8080/PDFFlow/Images/BankAccountStatementNextTransactionhistory.png" style="max-width:100%;"></a>
Fig. 12</p>
<p>In order to add the block, the method</p>
<ul>
<li>Adds the line and the "<em>Transaction history</em>" title using the <strong>AddStatementsHeadLine</strong> method;</li>
<li>Adds the statement table using the <strong>AddStatementsTable</strong> method;</li>
<li>Adds the "The Ending Daily Balance does ..." comment using the <strong>AddEndingDayBalanceComment</strong> method.</li>
</ul>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-addstatementsheadline-method" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-addstatementsheadline-method"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The AddStatementsHeadLine method</h6>
<p>The method adds the line and the paragraph with the "<em>Transaction history</em>" title to the section.</p>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-addstatementstable-method" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-addstatementstable-method"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The AddStatementsTable method</h6>
<p>The method creates the table with 6 columns and</p>
<ul>
<li>Adds the headers of table's columns using the <strong>AddStatementsHead</strong> method;</li>
<li>Creates the local variable of <strong>total</strong> of the <strong>Model.Statement</strong> class to count the totals of the transactions;</li>
<li>Adds the rows with transactions using the <strong>AddStatements</strong> method in which the properties of the <strong>total</strong> variable are changed;</li>
<li>Adds the row with totals of the transactions using the <strong>AddStatementsTotal</strong> method and passing it the <strong>total</strong> variable.</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>        <span class="pl-k">private</span> <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">AddStatementsTable</span>(<span class="pl-en">SectionBuilder</span> <span class="pl-smi">sectionBuilder</span>)
        {
            <span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-smi">tableBuilder</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">sectionBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddTable</span>();
            <span class="pl-smi">tableBuilder</span>
                .<span class="pl-en">SetBorder</span>(<span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">None</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">ApplyStyle</span>(
                    <span class="pl-smi">StyleBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">New</span>()
                    .<span class="pl-en">SetFont</span>(<span class="pl-smi">FNT7_2</span>)
                    )
                .<span class="pl-en">SetMarginBottom</span>(<span class="pl-c1">4</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">AddColumnPercentToTable</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-c1">4</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">AddColumnPercentToTable</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-c1">11</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">AddColumnPercentToTable</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-c1">48</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">AddColumnPercentToTable</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-c1">13</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">AddColumnPercentToTable</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-c1">13</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">AddColumnPercent</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-c1">11</span>);
            <span class="pl-en">AddStatementsHead</span>(<span class="pl-smi">tableBuilder</span>);
            <span class="pl-en">Statement</span> <span class="pl-smi">total</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-en">Statement</span>();
            <span class="pl-en">AddStatements</span>(<span class="pl-smi">tableBuilder</span>, <span class="pl-smi">total</span>);
            <span class="pl-en">AddStatementsTotal</span>(<span class="pl-smi">tableBuilder</span>, <span class="pl-smi">total</span>);
        }</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-addstatementshead-method" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-addstatementshead-method"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The AddStatementsHead method</h6>
<p>The method adds the <em>Statements</em> row to the table and sets it according to the design:</p>
<ul>
<li>sets the VerticalAlignment;</li>
<li>sets the bottom border;</li>
<li>adds the headers of the <em>Statements</em> columns.</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>        <span class="pl-k">private</span> <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">AddStatementsHead</span>(<span class="pl-en">TableBuilder</span> <span class="pl-smi">tableBuilder</span>)
        {
            <span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-smi">tableRowBuilder</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">tableBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddRow</span>();
            <span class="pl-smi">tableRowBuilder</span>
                .<span class="pl-en">SetFont</span>(<span class="pl-smi">FNT7_2</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">SetVerticalAlignment</span>(<span class="pl-smi">VerticalAlignment</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Bottom</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">SetBorder</span>(<span class="pl-smi">borderBuilder</span> <span class="pl-k">=&gt;</span>
                {
                    <span class="pl-smi">borderBuilder</span>
                        .<span class="pl-en">SetLeftBorder</span>(<span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">None</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Color</span>.<span class="pl-smi">None</span>)
                        .<span class="pl-en">SetTopBorder</span>(<span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">None</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Color</span>.<span class="pl-smi">None</span>)
                        .<span class="pl-en">SetRightBorder</span>(<span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">None</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Color</span>.<span class="pl-smi">None</span>)
                        .<span class="pl-en">SetBottomBorder</span>(<span class="pl-c1">0.5f</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Solid</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Color</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Black</span>);
                });
            <span class="pl-smi">tableRowBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddCell</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Date<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>).<span class="pl-en">SetPadding</span>(<span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">4</span>, <span class="pl-c1">4</span>);
            <span class="pl-smi">tableRowBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddCell</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Check<span class="pl-cce">\n</span>Number<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">SetHorizontalAlignment</span>(<span class="pl-smi">HorizontalAlignment</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Right</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">SetPadding</span>(<span class="pl-c1">4</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">4</span>, <span class="pl-c1">4</span>);
            <span class="pl-smi">tableRowBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddCell</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Description<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>).<span class="pl-en">SetPadding</span>(<span class="pl-c1">4</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">4</span>, <span class="pl-c1">4</span>);
            <span class="pl-smi">tableRowBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddCell</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Deposits/<span class="pl-cce">\n</span>Credits<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">SetHorizontalAlignment</span>(<span class="pl-smi">HorizontalAlignment</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Right</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">SetPadding</span>(<span class="pl-c1">4</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">4</span>, <span class="pl-c1">4</span>);
            <span class="pl-smi">tableRowBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddCell</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Withdrawals/<span class="pl-cce">\n</span>Debits<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">SetHorizontalAlignment</span>(<span class="pl-smi">HorizontalAlignment</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Right</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">SetPadding</span>(<span class="pl-c1">4</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">4</span>, <span class="pl-c1">4</span>);
            <span class="pl-smi">tableRowBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddCell</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Ending daily<span class="pl-cce">\n</span>balance<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">SetHorizontalAlignment</span>(<span class="pl-smi">HorizontalAlignment</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Right</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">SetPadding</span>(<span class="pl-c1">4</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">4</span>);
        }</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-addstatementshead-method-1" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-addstatementshead-method-1"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The AddStatementsHead method</h6>
<p>The method adds the row for each object of the <strong>Model.Statement</strong> class to the <em>Statements</em> table. The objects are in the list in the <strong>statements</strong> property.  The values of each <strong>Model.Statement</strong> object from the list are used to fill the cells of one row of the table.</p>
<p>The empty values of 0 and null must not be shown.
To do this, the value of each property is converted depending on its type. The conversion is performed using the methods:</p>
<ul>
<li>The <strong>Helper.ReplaceNullDate</strong> for the <em>DateTime</em> type;</li>
<li>The <strong>Helper.ReplaceNullStr</strong> for the <em>String</em> type;</li>
<li>The <strong>Helper.ReplaceZeroDouble</strong> for the <em>Double</em> type.</li>
</ul>
<p>When the rows are added, the properties of the <strong>total</strong> parameter are changed
to accumulate the values of the <strong>Deposits</strong> and <strong>Withdrawals</strong> properties.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>        <span class="pl-k">private</span> <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">AddStatements</span>(<span class="pl-en">TableBuilder</span> <span class="pl-smi">tableBuilder</span>, <span class="pl-en">Statement</span> <span class="pl-smi">total</span>)
        {
            <span class="pl-k">double</span> <span class="pl-smi">deposits</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
            <span class="pl-k">double</span> <span class="pl-smi">withdrawals</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
            <span class="pl-k">foreach</span> (<span class="pl-en">Statement</span> <span class="pl-smi">statement</span> <span class="pl-k">in</span> <span class="pl-smi">statements</span>)
            {
                <span class="pl-smi">deposits</span> <span class="pl-k">+=</span> <span class="pl-smi">statement</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Deposits</span>;
                <span class="pl-smi">withdrawals</span> <span class="pl-k">+=</span> <span class="pl-smi">statement</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Withdrawals</span>;
                <span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-smi">tableRowBuilder</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">tableBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddRow</span>();
                <span class="pl-smi">tableRowBuilder</span>
                    .<span class="pl-en">SetFont</span>(<span class="pl-smi">FNT7_2</span>)
                    .<span class="pl-en">SetVerticalAlignment</span>(<span class="pl-smi">VerticalAlignment</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Top</span>)
                    .<span class="pl-en">SetBorder</span>(<span class="pl-smi">borderBuilder</span> <span class="pl-k">=&gt;</span>
                    {
                        <span class="pl-smi">borderBuilder</span>
                            .<span class="pl-en">SetLeftStroke</span>(<span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">None</span>)
                            .<span class="pl-en">SetTopStroke</span>(<span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">None</span>)
                            .<span class="pl-en">SetRightStroke</span>(<span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">None</span>)
                            .<span class="pl-en">SetBottomBorder</span>(<span class="pl-c1">0.5f</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Solid</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Color</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Black</span>);
                    });
                <span class="pl-smi">tableRowBuilder</span>
                    .<span class="pl-en">AddCell</span>(<span class="pl-en">ReplaceNullDate</span>(<span class="pl-smi">statement</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Date</span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>M/d<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>))
                    .<span class="pl-en">SetPadding</span>(<span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">4</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>);
                <span class="pl-smi">tableRowBuilder</span>
                    .<span class="pl-en">AddCell</span>(<span class="pl-en">ReplaceNullStr</span>(<span class="pl-smi">statement</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Check</span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>))
                    .<span class="pl-en">SetHorizontalAlignment</span>(<span class="pl-smi">HorizontalAlignment</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Right</span>)
                    .<span class="pl-en">SetPadding</span>(<span class="pl-c1">4</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">4</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>);
                <span class="pl-smi">tableRowBuilder</span>
                    .<span class="pl-en">AddCell</span>(<span class="pl-en">ReplaceNullStr</span>(<span class="pl-smi">statement</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Details</span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>))
                    .<span class="pl-en">SetPadding</span>(<span class="pl-c1">4</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">4</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>);
                <span class="pl-smi">tableRowBuilder</span>
                    .<span class="pl-en">AddCell</span>(<span class="pl-en">ReplaceZeroDouble</span>(<span class="pl-smi">statement</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Deposits</span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>))
                    .<span class="pl-en">SetHorizontalAlignment</span>(<span class="pl-smi">HorizontalAlignment</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Right</span>)
                    .<span class="pl-en">SetPadding</span>(<span class="pl-c1">4</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">4</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>);
                <span class="pl-smi">tableRowBuilder</span>
                    .<span class="pl-en">AddCell</span>(<span class="pl-en">ReplaceZeroDouble</span>(<span class="pl-smi">statement</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Withdrawals</span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>))
                    .<span class="pl-en">SetHorizontalAlignment</span>(<span class="pl-smi">HorizontalAlignment</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Right</span>)
                    .<span class="pl-en">SetPadding</span>(<span class="pl-c1">4</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">4</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>);
                <span class="pl-smi">tableRowBuilder</span>
                    .<span class="pl-en">AddCell</span>(<span class="pl-en">ReplaceZeroDouble</span>(<span class="pl-smi">statement</span>.<span class="pl-smi">EndingDailyBalance</span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>))
                    .<span class="pl-en">SetHorizontalAlignment</span>(<span class="pl-smi">HorizontalAlignment</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Right</span>)
                    .<span class="pl-en">SetPadding</span>(<span class="pl-c1">4</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>);
            }
            <span class="pl-smi">total</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Deposits</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">Math</span>.<span class="pl-en">Round</span>(<span class="pl-smi">deposits</span>, <span class="pl-c1">2</span>, <span class="pl-smi">MidpointRounding</span>.<span class="pl-smi">ToEven</span>);
            <span class="pl-smi">total</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Withdrawals</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">Math</span>.<span class="pl-en">Round</span>(<span class="pl-smi">withdrawals</span>, <span class="pl-c1">2</span>, <span class="pl-smi">MidpointRounding</span>.<span class="pl-smi">ToEven</span>);
        }
</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-addstatementstotal-method" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-addstatementstotal-method"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The AddStatementsTotal method</h6>
<p>The method adds 2 last rows to the <em>Statements</em> table
These rows have the following features:</p>
<ul>
<li>the Bold font;</li>
<li>The first row contains only one value in the "Ending Balance" column that is filled from the <strong>statementInfo.EndingBalance</strong> property;</li>
<li>The second row contains 2 values in the "Deposits/Credits" и "Withdrawals/Debits" columns. These values contain in the <strong>total</strong> of the <strong>Deposits</strong> and <strong>Withdrawals</strong> properties.
The <strong>total</strong> parameter is passed to the method.</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>        <span class="pl-k">private</span> <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">AddStatementsTotal</span>(<span class="pl-en">TableBuilder</span> <span class="pl-smi">tableBuilder</span>, <span class="pl-en">Statement</span> <span class="pl-smi">total</span>)
        {
            <span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-smi">tableRowBuilder</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">tableBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddRow</span>();
            <span class="pl-smi">tableRowBuilder</span>
                .<span class="pl-en">SetFont</span>(<span class="pl-smi">FNT7_2B</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">SetVerticalAlignment</span>(<span class="pl-smi">VerticalAlignment</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Top</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">SetBorder</span>(<span class="pl-smi">borderBuilder</span> <span class="pl-k">=&gt;</span>
                {
                    <span class="pl-smi">borderBuilder</span>
                        .<span class="pl-en">SetLeftStroke</span>(<span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">None</span>)
                        .<span class="pl-en">SetTopStroke</span>(<span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">None</span>)
                        .<span class="pl-en">SetRightStroke</span>(<span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">None</span>)
                        .<span class="pl-en">SetBottomBorder</span>(<span class="pl-c1">2f</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Solid</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Color</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Black</span>);
                });
            <span class="pl-smi">tableRowBuilder</span>
                .<span class="pl-en">AddCell</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Ending balance on <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">+</span>
                            <span class="pl-smi">statementInfo</span>.<span class="pl-smi">DateEnd</span>.<span class="pl-en">ToString</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>M/d<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-smi">DocumentLocale</span>))
                .<span class="pl-en">SetPadding</span>(<span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">4</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">SetColSpan</span>(<span class="pl-c1">5</span>);
            <span class="pl-smi">tableRowBuilder</span>
                .<span class="pl-en">AddCell</span>(<span class="pl-en">ReplaceZeroDouble</span>(<span class="pl-smi">statementInfo</span>.<span class="pl-smi">EndingBalance</span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>))
                .<span class="pl-en">SetHorizontalAlignment</span>(<span class="pl-smi">HorizontalAlignment</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Right</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">SetPadding</span>(<span class="pl-c1">4</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>);
            <span class="pl-smi">tableRowBuilder</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">tableBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddRow</span>();
            <span class="pl-smi">tableRowBuilder</span>
                .<span class="pl-en">SetFont</span>(<span class="pl-smi">FNT7_2B</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">SetVerticalAlignment</span>(<span class="pl-smi">VerticalAlignment</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Top</span>);
            <span class="pl-smi">tableRowBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddCell</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Totals<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>).<span class="pl-en">SetPadding</span>(<span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">4</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>).<span class="pl-en">SetColSpan</span>(<span class="pl-c1">3</span>);
            <span class="pl-smi">tableRowBuilder</span>
                .<span class="pl-en">AddCell</span>(<span class="pl-en">ReplaceZeroDouble</span>(<span class="pl-smi">total</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Deposits</span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>$<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>))
                .<span class="pl-en">SetHorizontalAlignment</span>(<span class="pl-smi">HorizontalAlignment</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Right</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">SetPadding</span>(<span class="pl-c1">4</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">4</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>);
            <span class="pl-smi">tableRowBuilder</span>
                .<span class="pl-en">AddCell</span>(<span class="pl-en">ReplaceZeroDouble</span>(<span class="pl-smi">total</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Withdrawals</span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>$<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>))
                .<span class="pl-en">SetHorizontalAlignment</span>(<span class="pl-smi">HorizontalAlignment</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Right</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">SetPadding</span>(<span class="pl-c1">4</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">4</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>);
            <span class="pl-smi">tableRowBuilder</span>
                .<span class="pl-en">AddCell</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">SetHorizontalAlignment</span>(<span class="pl-smi">HorizontalAlignment</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Right</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">SetPadding</span>(<span class="pl-c1">4</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>);
        }
</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-addendingdaybalancecomment-method" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-addendingdaybalancecomment-method"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The AddEndingDayBalanceComment method</h6>
<p>The method adds the "<em>The Ending Daily Balance does not reflect...</em>" text below the table using the <strong>Helper.AddParagraph</strong> method that takes the object of the <strong>Gehtsoft.PDFFlow.Builder.SectionBuilder</strong> class as the parameter.</p>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-addservicefeesummary-method" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-addservicefeesummary-method"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The AddServiceFeeSummary method</h6>
<p>The method adds the "<strong>Service fee summary</strong>" block shown in Fig. 13.</p>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/1b8cd25c6d9cb3ba09f4f73168ccd02c4412874c12a5fb9547b66da503e6437d/687474703a2f2f7372762d646576302e67656874736f66742e636f6d3a383038302f504446466c6f772f496d616765732f42616e6b4163636f756e7453746174656d656e744e65787446656573756d6d6172792e706e67"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/1b8cd25c6d9cb3ba09f4f73168ccd02c4412874c12a5fb9547b66da503e6437d/687474703a2f2f7372762d646576302e67656874736f66742e636f6d3a383038302f504446466c6f772f496d616765732f42616e6b4163636f756e7453746174656d656e744e65787446656573756d6d6172792e706e67" alt="Fig. 13" title="Service fee summary" data-canonical-src="http://srv-dev0.gehtsoft.com:8080/PDFFlow/Images/BankAccountStatementNextFeesummary.png" style="max-width:100%;"></a>
Fig. 13</p>
<p>The block consists of</p>
<ul>
<li>The text paragraph with the "<em>Monthly service fee summary</em>" title;</li>
<li>The fee table.</li>
</ul>
<p>To create this block, the method uses</p>
<ul>
<li>The AddServiceFeeSummaryParagrpaph method;</li>
<li>The AddServiceFeeSummaryTable method.</li>
</ul>
<p>The last row of the table is not included in the second page due to the number of items in the <em>Statements</em> list.
The library creates the additional page automatically. Also, it adds the Title that has been added using the <strong>Gehtsoft.PDFFlow.Builder.SectionBuilder.AddHeaderToBothPages</strong> method.
Therefore, the sample program does not need to control the creation of additional pages.</p>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-addservicefeesummaryparagrpaph-method" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-addservicefeesummaryparagrpaph-method"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The AddServiceFeeSummaryParagrpaph method</h6>
<p>The method adds to the page:</p>
<ul>
<li>The paragraph with the "<em>Monthly service fee summary</em>" title;</li>
<li>The paragraph with text.</li>
</ul>
<p>The method sets the paragraph since the URL is added to it.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>        <span class="pl-k">private</span> <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">AddServiceFeeSummaryParagrpaph</span>(<span class="pl-en">SectionBuilder</span> <span class="pl-smi">sectionBuilder</span>)
        {
            <span class="pl-en">AddParagraph</span>(<span class="pl-smi">sectionBuilder</span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Monthly service fee summary<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-smi">FNT7_9B</span>, <span class="pl-c1">4.8f</span>);
            <span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-smi">paragraphBuilder</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">sectionBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddParagraph</span>(); 
            <span class="pl-smi">paragraphBuilder</span>
                .<span class="pl-en">SetUrlStyle</span>(
                    <span class="pl-smi">StyleBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">New</span>()
                        .<span class="pl-en">SetFont</span>(<span class="pl-smi">FNT7_2URL</span>)
                        .<span class="pl-en">SetBorder</span>(<span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">None</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Color</span>.<span class="pl-smi">White</span>)
                    )
                .<span class="pl-en">SetFont</span>(<span class="pl-smi">FNT7_2</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">AddTextToParagraph</span>(
                    <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>For a complete list of fees and detailed account information, please see the <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">+</span> 
                    <span class="pl-smi">statementInfo</span>.<span class="pl-smi">BankName</span> <span class="pl-k">+</span> 
                    <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> Fee and Information Schedule and Account Agreement applicable to your account or talk to a banker. Go to <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
                    )
                .<span class="pl-en">AddUrlToParagraph</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>https://<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">+</span> 
                    <span class="pl-smi">statementInfo</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Online</span> <span class="pl-k">+</span> 
                    <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>/feefaq<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-smi">statementInfo</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Online</span> <span class="pl-k">+</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>/feefaq<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">AddTextToParagraph</span>(
                    <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> to find answers to common questions about the monthly service fee on your account.<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);
        }
</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-addservicefeesummarytable-method" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-addservicefeesummarytable-method"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The AddServiceFeeSummaryTable method</h6>
<p>The method creates the table with 4 columns. The last column is for the checkbox in the "Average ledger balance " row.
The rows are added to the table using the <strong>AddTableRows</strong> method that is passed the rows as the array of the objects of the <strong>RowData</strong> inner class. The rows are created using the <strong>GetServiceFeeSummaryRowData</strong> method.
The row numbers with bottom border is the last parameter passed to the <strong>AddTableRows</strong> method. These are #0 and #2 rows.</p>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-internal-rowdata-class" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-internal-rowdata-class"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The internal RowData class</h6>
<p>The object of this class contains</p>
<ul>
<li>The <strong>data</strong> array of the strings;</li>
<li>The <strong>font</strong> array of fonts with one font for each string.</li>
</ul>
<p>Also, the class defines:</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p>The <strong>virtual</strong> <strong>GetLength</strong> method using to define the number of the rows;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>The <strong>virtual</strong> <strong>AddTextToParagraph</strong> method using to add the rows to the table;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>The <strong>virtual</strong> <strong>BottomBorderWidth</strong> method using to define the bottom border width of the row;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>The <strong>virtual</strong> <strong>BottomBorderStroke</strong>  method to define the bottom border style of the row.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-internal-bottomborderrowdata-class" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-internal-bottomborderrowdata-class"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The internal BottomBorderRowData class</h6>
<p>This class extends the <strong>RowData class</strong> for the rows with the bottom borders.</p>
<p>This class overrides the methods:</p>
<ul>
<li>The <strong>AddTextToParagraph</strong>;</li>
<li>The <strong>BottomBorderWidth</strong>;</li>
<li>The <strong>BottomBorderStroke</strong>.</li>
</ul>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-internal-complexrowdata-class" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-internal-complexrowdata-class"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The internal ComplexRowData class</h6>
<p>This class extends the <strong>RowData class</strong> for the rows with different fonts such as</p>
<ul>
<li>"Have any <strong>ONE</strong> of the following account requirements";</li>
<li>CHECK_BOX + "Online only statements ($5.00 discount)".</li>
</ul>
<p>The class overrides the methods:</p>
<ul>
<li>The <strong>GetLength</strong>;</li>
<li>The <strong>AddTextToParagraph</strong>.</li>
</ul>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-getservicefeesummaryrowdata-method" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-getservicefeesummaryrowdata-method"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The GetServiceFeeSummaryRowData method</h6>
<p>The method prepares the data to fill the rows of <em>ServiceFeeSummary</em> table.
The method creates the objects of the <strong>RowData</strong> array with the values for the <em>ServiceFeeSummary</em> table using the <strong>statementInfo</strong> property.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>        <span class="pl-k">private</span> <span class="pl-en">RowData</span>[] <span class="pl-en">GetServiceFeeSummaryRowData</span>()
        {
            <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-en">RowData</span>[]
                {
                    <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-en">RowData</span>(
                        <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Fee period <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">+</span> 
                        <span class="pl-smi">statementInfo</span>.<span class="pl-smi">DateBegin</span>.<span class="pl-en">ToString</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>MM/dd/yyyy<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-smi">DocumentLocale</span>) <span class="pl-k">+</span> 
                        <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> - <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">+</span> 
                        <span class="pl-smi">statementInfo</span>.<span class="pl-smi">DateEnd</span>.<span class="pl-en">ToString</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>MM/dd/yyyy<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-smi">DocumentLocale</span>),
                        <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Standard monthly service fee <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">+</span> 
                        <span class="pl-en">ReplaceZeroDouble</span>(<span class="pl-smi">statementInfo</span>.<span class="pl-smi">StandartServiceFee</span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>$0.00<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>$<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>),
                        <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>You paid <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">+</span> 
                        <span class="pl-en">ReplaceZeroDouble</span>(<span class="pl-smi">statementInfo</span>.<span class="pl-smi">ServiceFee</span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>$0.00<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>$<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>)
                    ),
                    <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-en">RowData</span>(
                        <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-en">FontBuilder</span>[] {
                            <span class="pl-smi">FNT7_2B</span>,
                            <span class="pl-smi">FNT7_2</span>
                        },
                        <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>How to reduce the monthly service fee by <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">+</span> 
                        <span class="pl-en">ReplaceZeroDouble</span>(<span class="pl-smi">statementInfo</span>.<span class="pl-smi">ServiceDiscount</span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>$0.00<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>$<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>),
                        <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Minimum required<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
                        <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>This fee period<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
                    ),
                    <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-en">ComplexRowData</span>(
                        <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-en">RowData</span> (
                                <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-en">FontBuilder</span>[] {
                                    <span class="pl-smi">FNT7_2</span>,
                                    <span class="pl-smi">FNT7_2B</span>,
                                    <span class="pl-smi">FNT7_2</span>
                                },
                                <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Have any <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
                                <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>ONE<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
                                <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> of the following account requirements<span class="pl-cce">\n</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">+</span> 
                                <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Average ledger balance<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
                        ),
                        <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-en">FontBuilder</span>[] {
                            <span class="pl-smi">FNT7_2</span>,
                            <span class="pl-smi">FNT7_2</span>,
                            <span class="pl-smi">FNTZ8</span>
                        },
                        <span class="pl-en">ReplaceZeroDouble</span>(<span class="pl-smi">statementInfo</span>.<span class="pl-smi">MinimumRequired</span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>$0.00<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>$<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>),
                        <span class="pl-en">ReplaceZeroDouble</span>(<span class="pl-smi">Math</span>.<span class="pl-en">Round</span>(<span class="pl-smi">statementInfo</span>.<span class="pl-smi">AverageBalance</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>, 
                        <span class="pl-smi">MidpointRounding</span>.<span class="pl-smi">ToEven</span>), <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>$0.00<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>$<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>),
                        <span class="pl-smi">CHECK_BOX</span>
                    ),
                    <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-en">RowData</span>(
                        <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-en">FontBuilder</span>[] {
                            <span class="pl-smi">FNT7_2B</span>
                        },
                        <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Monthly service fee discount(s) (applied when box is checked)<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
                    ),
                    <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-en">ComplexRowData</span>(
                        <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-en">RowData</span> (
                                <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-en">FontBuilder</span>[] {
                                    <span class="pl-smi">FNTZ8</span>,
                                    <span class="pl-smi">FNT7_2</span>
                                },
                                <span class="pl-smi">CHECK_BOX</span>,
                                <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> Online only statements (<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">+</span>
                                <span class="pl-en">ReplaceZeroDouble</span>(<span class="pl-smi">statementInfo</span>.<span class="pl-smi">ServiceDiscount</span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>$0.00<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>$<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>) <span class="pl-k">+</span> 
                                <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>  discount)<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
                        ),
                        <span class="pl-en">ReplaceZeroDouble</span>(<span class="pl-smi">statementInfo</span>.<span class="pl-smi">MinimumRequired</span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>$0.00<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>$<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>),
                        <span class="pl-en">ReplaceZeroDouble</span>(<span class="pl-smi">Math</span>.<span class="pl-en">Round</span>(<span class="pl-smi">statementInfo</span>.<span class="pl-smi">AverageBalance</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>, 
                            <span class="pl-smi">MidpointRounding</span>.<span class="pl-smi">ToEven</span>), <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>$0.00<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>$<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>)
                    )
                };
        }
</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-addtablerows-method" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-addtablerows-method"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The AddTableRows method</h6>
<p>The method adds the rows to the <em>ServiceFeeSummary</em> table using the passed array of the objects of the <strong>RowData</strong> class.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>        <span class="pl-k">private</span> <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">AddTableRows</span>(<span class="pl-en">TableBuilder</span> <span class="pl-smi">tableBuilder</span>, <span class="pl-en">RowData</span>[] <span class="pl-smi">rows</span>, 
            <span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-smi">columnCount</span>, <span class="pl-k">params</span> <span class="pl-k">int</span>[] <span class="pl-smi">underlines</span>)
        {
            <span class="pl-k">for</span>(<span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-smi">i</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-smi">l</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">rows</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Length</span>; <span class="pl-smi">i</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span> <span class="pl-smi">l</span>; <span class="pl-smi">i</span><span class="pl-k">++</span>) 
            {
                <span class="pl-en">RowData</span> <span class="pl-smi">row</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">rows</span>[<span class="pl-smi">i</span>];
                <span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-smi">tableRowBuilder</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">tableBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddRow</span>();
                <span class="pl-smi">tableRowBuilder</span>
                    .<span class="pl-en">SetBorder</span>(<span class="pl-smi">borderBuilder</span> <span class="pl-k">=&gt;</span>
                    {
                        <span class="pl-smi">borderBuilder</span>
                            .<span class="pl-en">SetLeftBorder</span>(<span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">None</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Color</span>.<span class="pl-smi">None</span>)
                            .<span class="pl-en">SetTopBorder</span>(<span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">None</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Color</span>.<span class="pl-smi">None</span>)
                            .<span class="pl-en">SetRightBorder</span>(<span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">None</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Color</span>.<span class="pl-smi">None</span>);
                        <span class="pl-k">if</span> (<span class="pl-smi">underlines</span>.<span class="pl-en">Contains</span>(<span class="pl-smi">i</span>))
                        {
                            <span class="pl-smi">borderBuilder</span>
                                .<span class="pl-en">SetBottomBorder</span>(<span class="pl-c1">0.5f</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Solid</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Color</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Black</span>);
                        } <span class="pl-k">else</span>
                        {
                            <span class="pl-smi">borderBuilder</span>
                                .<span class="pl-en">SetBottomBorder</span>(<span class="pl-smi">row</span>.<span class="pl-en">BottomBorderWidth</span>(), 
                                    <span class="pl-smi">row</span>.<span class="pl-en">BottomBorderStroke</span>(), <span class="pl-smi">Color</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Black</span>);
                        }
                    });
                <span class="pl-k">for</span>(<span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-smi">j</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>; <span class="pl-smi">j</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span> <span class="pl-smi">columnCount</span>; <span class="pl-smi">j</span><span class="pl-k">++</span>)
                {
                    <span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">tableRowBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddCell</span>();
                    <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>
                        .<span class="pl-en">SetHorizontalAlignment</span>(<span class="pl-smi">j</span> <span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span> <span class="pl-k">?</span> 
                            <span class="pl-smi">HorizontalAlignment</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Right</span> <span class="pl-k">:</span> 
                            <span class="pl-smi">HorizontalAlignment</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Left</span>)
                        .<span class="pl-en">SetVerticalAlignment</span>(<span class="pl-smi">VerticalAlignment</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Bottom</span>);
                    <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>
                        .<span class="pl-en">SetPadding</span>(<span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>);
                    <span class="pl-k">if</span> (<span class="pl-smi">j</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span> <span class="pl-smi">row</span>.<span class="pl-en">GetLength</span>())
                    {
                        <span class="pl-smi">row</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddTextToParagraph</span>(<span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddParagraph</span>(), <span class="pl-smi">j</span>);
                    } <span class="pl-k">else</span>
                    {
                        <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>
                            .<span class="pl-en">SetFont</span>(<span class="pl-smi">row</span>.<span class="pl-en">GetLastFont</span>())
                            .<span class="pl-en">AddParagraphToCell</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-addtransactionfeesummary-method" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-addtransactionfeesummary-method"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The AddTransactionFeeSummary method</h6>
