<p>The method adds the "<strong>Transaction fee summary</strong>" block shown in Fig. 14.</p>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/50dfc3fc671a75c2d733421ffb24c75ab7105ac126dd916cdbbb261f5e4725df/687474703a2f2f7372762d646576302e67656874736f66742e636f6d3a383038302f504446466c6f772f496d616765732f42616e6b4163636f756e7453746174656d656e744e6578745365727669636566656573756d6d617279312e706e67"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/50dfc3fc671a75c2d733421ffb24c75ab7105ac126dd916cdbbb261f5e4725df/687474703a2f2f7372762d646576302e67656874736f66742e636f6d3a383038302f504446466c6f772f496d616765732f42616e6b4163636f756e7453746174656d656e744e6578745365727669636566656573756d6d617279312e706e67" alt="Fig. 14" title="Transaction fee summary" data-canonical-src="http://srv-dev0.gehtsoft.com:8080/PDFFlow/Images/BankAccountStatementNextServicefeesummary1.png" style="max-width:100%;"></a> Fig. 14</p>
<p>The block consists of</p>
<ul>
<li>the line;</li>
<li>the paragraph with the "<em>Account transaction fees summary</em>" title;</li>
<li>the fee table;</li>
<li>the line;</li>
<li>the paragraph with the "<em>Your feedback matters...</em>" checkbox.</li>
</ul>
<p>To create the block, the method uses</p>
<ul>
<li>The <strong>AddTransactionFeeSummaryParagrpaph</strong> method;</li>
<li>The <strong>AddTransactionFeeSummaryTable</strong> method;</li>
<li>The <strong>Gehtsoft.PDFFlow.Builder.SectionBuilder.AddLine</strong> method;</li>
<li>The <strong>AddYourFeedBack</strong> method.</li>
</ul>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-addtransactionfeesummaryparagrpaph-method" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-addtransactionfeesummaryparagrpaph-method"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The AddTransactionFeeSummaryParagrpaph method</h6>
<p>The method</p>
<ul>
<li>Adds the line using the <strong>Gehtsoft.PDFFlow.Builder.SectionBuilder.AddLine</strong> method;</li>
<li>Adds the paragraph with title using the <strong>Helper.AddParagraph</strong> method that takes the object of the <strong>Gehtsoft.PDFFlow.Builder.SectionBuilder</strong> class as the parameter.</li>
</ul>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-addtransactionfeesummarytable-method" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-addtransactionfeesummarytable-method"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The AddTransactionFeeSummaryTable method</h6>
<p>The method creates the table with 6 columns.
The rows are added to the table using the <strong>AddTableRows</strong> method that is passed the rows as the array of the objects of the <strong>RowData</strong> inner class. The rows are created using the <strong>GetTransactionFeeSummaryRowData</strong> method.</p>
<p>The row numbers with bottom border is the last parameter passed to the <strong>AddTableRows</strong> method. This is #0 row.</p>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-gettransactionfeesummaryrowdata-method" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-gettransactionfeesummaryrowdata-method"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The GetTransactionFeeSummaryRowData method</h6>
<p>The method creates the data to fill the rows of the <em>TransactionFeeSummary</em> table.
The method creates the objects of the <strong>RowData</strong> array with the values for the <em>TransactionFeeSummary</em> table using the <strong>statementInfo</strong> property.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>        <span class="pl-k">private</span> <span class="pl-en">RowData</span>[] <span class="pl-en">GetTransactionFeeSummaryRowData</span>()
        {
            <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-en">RowData</span>[]
                {
                    <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-en">RowData</span>(
                        <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Service charge description<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
                        <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Units used<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
                        <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Units included<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
                        <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Excess units<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
                        <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Service charge per<span class="pl-cce">\n</span>excess units ($)<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
                        <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Total service<span class="pl-cce">\n</span>charge ($)<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
                    ),
                    <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-en">BottomBorderRowData</span>(
                        <span class="pl-c1">2f</span>,
                        <span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Solid</span>,
                        <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Transactions<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
                        <span class="pl-en">ReplaceZeroInt</span>(<span class="pl-smi">statementInfo</span>.<span class="pl-smi">TransactionUnits</span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>0<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>),
                        <span class="pl-en">ReplaceZeroInt</span>(<span class="pl-smi">statementInfo</span>.<span class="pl-smi">TransactionUnitsIncluded</span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>0<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>),
                        <span class="pl-en">ReplaceZeroInt</span>(<span class="pl-smi">statementInfo</span>.<span class="pl-smi">TransactionExcessUnits</span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>0<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>),
                        <span class="pl-en">ReplaceZeroDouble</span>(<span class="pl-smi">statementInfo</span>.<span class="pl-smi">ServiceCharge</span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>0.00<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>),
                        <span class="pl-en">ReplaceZeroDouble</span>(<span class="pl-smi">statementInfo</span>.<span class="pl-smi">TotalServiceCharge</span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>0.00<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>)
                    ),
                    <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-en">RowData</span>(
                        <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-en">FontBuilder</span>[] {
                            <span class="pl-smi">FNT7_2B</span>
                        },
                        <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Total service charges<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
                        <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
                        <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
                        <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
                        <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
                        <span class="pl-en">ReplaceZeroDouble</span>(<span class="pl-smi">statementInfo</span>.<span class="pl-smi">TotalServiceCharge</span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>$0.00<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>$<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>)
                    )
                };
        }</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-addyourfeedback-method" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-addyourfeedback-method"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The AddYourFeedBack method</h6>
<p>The method adds the table with 2 rows to the page.
The checkbox is added to the left column.
The text beginning with "<em>Your feedback matters</em>" is added to the right column.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>        <span class="pl-k">private</span> <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">AddYourFeedBack</span>(<span class="pl-en">SectionBuilder</span> <span class="pl-smi">sectionBuilder</span>)
        {
            <span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-smi">tableBuilder</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">sectionBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddTable</span>();
            <span class="pl-smi">tableBuilder</span>
                .<span class="pl-en">SetBorder</span>(<span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">None</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">SetContentRowBorderWidth</span>(<span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">ApplyStyle</span>(
                    <span class="pl-smi">StyleBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">New</span>()
                    .<span class="pl-en">SetHorizontalAlignment</span>(<span class="pl-smi">HorizontalAlignment</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Left</span>)
                    )
                .<span class="pl-en">SetMarginTop</span>(<span class="pl-c1">10</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">SetWidth</span>(<span class="pl-smi">XUnit</span>.<span class="pl-en">FromPercent</span>(<span class="pl-c1">54</span>))
                .<span class="pl-en">AddColumnPercentToTable</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-c1">7</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">AddColumnPercent</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-c1">93</span>);
            <span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-smi">tableRowBuilder</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">tableBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddRow</span>();
            <span class="pl-smi">tableRowBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddCell</span>(<span class="pl-smi">CHECK_BOX</span>).<span class="pl-en">SetFont</span>(<span class="pl-smi">FNTZ8</span>);
            <span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">tableRowBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddCell</span>();
            <span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-smi">paragraphBuilder</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddParagraph</span>();
            <span class="pl-smi">paragraphBuilder</span>
                .<span class="pl-en">SetUrlStyle</span>(
                    <span class="pl-smi">StyleBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">New</span>().<span class="pl-en">SetFont</span>(<span class="pl-smi">FNT7_5URL</span>)
                 )
                .<span class="pl-en">AddTextToParagraph</span>(
                    <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Your feedback matters<span class="pl-cce">\n</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-smi">FNT7_9B</span>
                )
                .<span class="pl-en">AddTextToParagraph</span>(
                    <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Share your compliments and complaints so we can better serve you.<span class="pl-cce">\n</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">+</span> 
                    <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Call us at <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">+</span> 
                    <span class="pl-smi">statementInfo</span>.<span class="pl-smi">FeedBackPhone</span> <span class="pl-k">+</span> 
                    <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>(<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">+</span> <span class="pl-smi">statementInfo</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Phone</span> <span class="pl-k">+</span> 
                    <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>) or visit <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
                    <span class="pl-smi">FNT7_5</span>
                )
                .<span class="pl-en">AddUrlToParagraph</span>(
                    <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>https://<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">+</span> 
                    <span class="pl-smi">statementInfo</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Online</span> <span class="pl-k">+</span> 
                    <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>/feedback<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, 
                    <span class="pl-smi">statementInfo</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Online</span> <span class="pl-k">+</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>/feedback<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
                    )
                .<span class="pl-en">AddTextToParagraph</span>(
                    <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>.<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
                    <span class="pl-smi">FNT7_5</span>
                );
        }
</pre></div>
<h4><a id="user-content-9-the-bankaccountstatementlastpagebuilder-class" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#9-the-bankaccountstatementlastpagebuilder-class"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>9. The BankAccountStatementLastPageBuilder class</h4>
<p>The <strong>BankAccountStatementLastPageBuilder.Build method</strong> performs responsibilities to</p>
<ul>
<li>Create the page and set its parameters;</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>            <span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-smi">sectionBuilder</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">documentBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddSection</span>();
            <span class="pl-smi">sectionBuilder</span>
                .<span class="pl-en">SetOrientation</span>(<span class="pl-smi">Orientation</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">SetMargins</span>(<span class="pl-smi">Margins</span>);</pre></div>
<ul>
<li>Create the header without the bank name;</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>            <span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-smi">headerBuilder</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">sectionBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddHeaderToBothPages</span>(<span class="pl-c1">80</span>);
            <span class="pl-en">AddTitle</span>(<span class="pl-smi">headerBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddTable</span>()
                , <span class="pl-c1">20f</span>, <span class="pl-c1">4</span>, <span class="pl-smi">AddCommonPageTitle</span>);</pre></div>
<ul>
<li>Add the line separating the header from the rest of the page content;</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>            <span class="pl-smi">headerBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddLine</span>(<span class="pl-smi">PageWidth</span>, <span class="pl-c1">2f</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Solid</span>);</pre></div>
<ul>
<li>Create the footer "©2020 SampleBank , N.A. All rights reserved. Member FDIC.";</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>            <span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-smi">footerBuilder</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">sectionBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddFooterToBothPages</span>(<span class="pl-c1">8</span>);
            <span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-smi">paragraphBuilder</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">footerBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddParagraph</span>();
            <span class="pl-smi">paragraphBuilder</span>
                .<span class="pl-en">SetAlignment</span>(<span class="pl-smi">HorizontalAlignment</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Left</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">SetFont</span>(<span class="pl-smi">FNT5_6</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">AddTextToParagraph</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>©2020 <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">+</span> <span class="pl-smi">statementInfo</span>.<span class="pl-smi">BankName</span> <span class="pl-k">+</span> 
                    <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> , <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">+</span> <span class="pl-smi">statementInfo</span>.<span class="pl-smi">BankNameState</span> <span class="pl-k">+</span> 
                    <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> All rights reserved. Member FDIC.<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);</pre></div>
<ul>
<li>Add the "<strong>Polices</strong>" block as the second header;</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>            <span class="pl-smi">headerBuilder</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">sectionBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddHeaderToBothPages</span>(<span class="pl-c1">90</span>);
            <span class="pl-en">AddGeneralStatementPolicies</span>(<span class="pl-smi">headerBuilder</span>);</pre></div>
<ul>
<li>Add the line separating the "<strong>Polices</strong>" from the rest of the page content;</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>            <span class="pl-smi">headerBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddLine</span>(<span class="pl-smi">PageWidth</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0.5f</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Solid</span>);</pre></div>
<ul>
<li>Add the "Instructions" and "Balance calculation" blocks.</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>            <span class="pl-en">AddAccountBalanceCalculationWorksheet</span>(<span class="pl-smi">sectionBuilder</span>);</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-addgeneralstatementpolicies-methods" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-addgeneralstatementpolicies-methods"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The AddGeneralStatementPolicies methods</h6>
<p>The method adds the "<strong>Polices</strong>" block shown in Fig. 15.</p>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/661395295fc311cb99c8bca1b341b03b7212c7ef49c2dc33288f7028074d33c1/687474703a2f2f7372762d646576302e67656874736f66742e636f6d3a383038302f504446466c6f772f496d616765732f42616e6b4163636f756e7453746174656d656e744c617374506f6c696365732e706e67"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/661395295fc311cb99c8bca1b341b03b7212c7ef49c2dc33288f7028074d33c1/687474703a2f2f7372762d646576302e67656874736f66742e636f6d3a383038302f504446466c6f772f496d616765732f42616e6b4163636f756e7453746174656d656e744c617374506f6c696365732e706e67" alt="Fig. 15" title="Polices" data-canonical-src="http://srv-dev0.gehtsoft.com:8080/PDFFlow/Images/BankAccountStatementLastPolices.png" style="max-width:100%;"></a> Fig. 15</p>
<p>The method adds the paragraph with the "<em>General statement policies for SampleBank</em>" title using the <strong>Helper.AddParagraph</strong> method that takes the parameter of the <strong>Gehtsoft.PDFFlow.Builder.RepeatingAreaBuilder</strong> class.</p>
<p>When the method adds the table filled by the <strong>FillGeneralStatementPoliciesTable</strong> method.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>        <span class="pl-k">private</span> <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">AddGeneralStatementPolicies</span>(<span class="pl-en">RepeatingAreaBuilder</span> <span class="pl-smi">builder</span>)
        {
            <span class="pl-en">AddParagraph</span>(
                <span class="pl-smi">builder</span>,
                <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>General statement policies for <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">+</span> <span class="pl-smi">statementInfo</span>.<span class="pl-smi">BankName</span>,
                <span class="pl-smi">FNT11_B</span>
            );
            <span class="pl-smi">builder</span>
                .<span class="pl-en">AddTableToRepeatingArea</span>(<span class="pl-smi">FillGeneralStatementPoliciesTable</span>);
        }
</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-fillgeneralstatementpoliciestable-method" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-fillgeneralstatementpoliciestable-method"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The FillGeneralStatementPoliciesTable method</h6>
<p>The method adds 2 columns and one row to the table and adds the <strong>Polices</strong> text to 2 cells of the row.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>        <span class="pl-k">private</span> <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">FillGeneralStatementPoliciesTable</span>(<span class="pl-en">TableBuilder</span> <span class="pl-smi">tableBuilder</span>)
        {
            <span class="pl-smi">tableBuilder</span>
                .<span class="pl-en">SetBorder</span>(<span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">None</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">SetMarginTop</span>(<span class="pl-c1">10</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">SetMarginBottom</span>(<span class="pl-c1">6</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">SetWidth</span>(<span class="pl-smi">XUnit</span>.<span class="pl-en">FromPercent</span>(<span class="pl-c1">100</span>))
                .<span class="pl-en">AddColumnPercentToTable</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-c1">50</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">AddColumnPercent</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-c1">50</span>);
            <span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-smi">tableRowBuilder</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">tableBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddRow</span>();
            <span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-smi">paragraphBuilder</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">tableRowBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddCell</span>().<span class="pl-en">AddParagraph</span>();
            <span class="pl-smi">paragraphBuilder</span>
                .<span class="pl-en">AddTextToParagraph</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Notice<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-smi">FNT7_2B</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">AddTextToParagraph</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>: <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">+</span>
                <span class="pl-smi">statementInfo</span>.<span class="pl-smi">BankName</span> <span class="pl-k">+</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>, <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">+</span>
                <span class="pl-smi">statementInfo</span>.<span class="pl-smi">BankNameState</span> <span class="pl-k">+</span>
                <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> may furnish information about accounts belonging to individuals, including sole proprietorships, to consumer reporting agencies.  If this applies to you, you have the right to dispute the accuracy of information that we have reported by writing to us at: <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
                <span class="pl-k">+</span> <span class="pl-smi">statementInfo</span>.<span class="pl-smi">ReportAddress</span> <span class="pl-k">+</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>.<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
                <span class="pl-smi">FNT7_2</span>);
            <span class="pl-smi">tableRowBuilder</span>
                .<span class="pl-en">AddCell</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>You must describe the specific information that is inaccurate or in dispute and the basis for any dispute with supporting documentation.  In the case of information that relates to an identity theft, you will need to provide us with an identity theft report.<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">SetFont</span>(<span class="pl-smi">FNT7_2</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">SetPadding</span>(<span class="pl-c1">8</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>);
        }
</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-addaccountbalancecalculationworksheet-method" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-addaccountbalancecalculationworksheet-method"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The AddAccountBalanceCalculationWorksheet method</h6>
<p>The method adds the "<strong>Instructions</strong>" and the "<strong>Balance calculation</strong>" blocks to the page. See Fig. 16.</p>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/bfb5b8601f1b73f9abfa925420e7ee47317093868f41dd4962f7852c91ce60e7/687474703a2f2f7372762d646576302e67656874736f66742e636f6d3a383038302f504446466c6f772f496d616765732f42616e6b4163636f756e7453746174656d656e744c617374576f726b73686565742e706e67"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/bfb5b8601f1b73f9abfa925420e7ee47317093868f41dd4962f7852c91ce60e7/687474703a2f2f7372762d646576302e67656874736f66742e636f6d3a383038302f504446466c6f772f496d616765732f42616e6b4163636f756e7453746174656d656e744c617374576f726b73686565742e706e67" alt="Fig. 16" title="Polices" data-canonical-src="http://srv-dev0.gehtsoft.com:8080/PDFFlow/Images/BankAccountStatementLastWorksheet.png" style="max-width:100%;"></a> Fig. 16</p>
<p>The block is the part of the page with 2 columns.
Therefore, the method uses</p>
<ul>
<li>The <strong>Gehtsoft.PDFFlow.Builder.SectionBuilder.AddRptAreaLeftToBothPages</strong> to add the left column with the "<strong>Instructions</strong>" block;</li>
<li>The <strong>Gehtsoft.PDFFlow.Builder.SectionBuilder.AddRptAreaRightToBothPages</strong> to add the right column with the "<strong>Balance calculation</strong> block.</li>
</ul>
<p>The columns are filled using the <strong>AddInstructions</strong> and <strong>AddBalanceCalc</strong> methods respectively.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>        <span class="pl-k">private</span> <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">AddAccountBalanceCalculationWorksheet</span>(<span class="pl-en">SectionBuilder</span> <span class="pl-smi">sectionBuilder</span>)
        {
            <span class="pl-k">float</span> <span class="pl-smi">repAreaWidth</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">PageWidth</span> <span class="pl-k">*</span> <span class="pl-c1">0.5f</span> <span class="pl-k">-</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span>;
            <span class="pl-smi">sectionBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddRptAreaLeftToBothPages</span>(<span class="pl-smi">repAreaWidth</span>, <span class="pl-smi">AddInstructions</span>);
            <span class="pl-smi">sectionBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddRptAreaRightToBothPages</span>(<span class="pl-smi">repAreaWidth</span>, <span class="pl-smi">AddBalanceCalc</span>);
        }
</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-addinstructions-method" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-addinstructions-method"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The AddInstructions method</h6>
<p>The method adds</p>
<ul>
<li>The common text with the "<em>Account Balance Calculation Worksheet</em>" title using the <strong>AddAboutAccountBalanceCalculationWorksheet</strong> method;</li>
<li>The instruction with the "<em>ENTER</em>" title using the <strong>AddInstuctionAboutENTER</strong> method;</li>
<li>The instruction with the "<em>ADD</em>" title using the <strong>AddInstuctionAboutADD</strong> method;</li>
<li>The instruction with the "<em>SUBTRACT</em>" title using the <strong>AddInstuctionAboutSUBTRACT</strong> method.</li>
</ul>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-addaboutaccountbalancecalculationworksheet-method" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-addaboutaccountbalancecalculationworksheet-method"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The AddAboutAccountBalanceCalculationWorksheet method</h6>
<p>The method adds the paragraph with the "<em>Account Balance Calculation Worksheet</em>" title using the <strong>Helper.AddParagraph</strong> method that takes the parameter of the <strong>Gehtsoft.PDFFlow.Builder.RepeatingAreaBuilder</strong> class.</p>
<p>The method adds the numbered list using the <strong>Helper.AddNumberedListToParagraph</strong> method. It passes the array of the items using the <strong>GetAboutAccountBalanceCalculationItems</strong> method.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>        <span class="pl-k">private</span> <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">AddAboutAccountBalanceCalculationWorksheet</span>(
            <span class="pl-en">RepeatingAreaBuilder</span> <span class="pl-smi">builder</span>)
        {
            <span class="pl-en">AddParagraph</span>(
                <span class="pl-smi">builder</span>,
                <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Account Balance Calculation Worksheet<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
                <span class="pl-smi">FNT11_B</span>
            );
            <span class="pl-k">string</span>[] <span class="pl-smi">items</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-en">GetAboutAccountBalanceCalculationItems</span>();
            <span class="pl-en">AddNumberedListToParagraph</span>(
                <span class="pl-smi">builder</span>,
                <span class="pl-smi">items</span>,
                <span class="pl-smi">FNT7_2</span>,
                <span class="pl-c1">14</span>
            );
        }
</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-getaboutaccountbalancecalculationitems-method" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-getaboutaccountbalancecalculationitems-method"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The GetAboutAccountBalanceCalculationItems method</h6>
<p>The method creates the array of the the rows.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>        <span class="pl-k">private</span> <span class="pl-k">string</span>[] <span class="pl-en">GetAboutAccountBalanceCalculationItems</span>()
        {
            <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-k">string</span>[]
            {
                <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Use the following worksheet to calculate your overall account balance.<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
                <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Go through your register and mark each check, withdrawal, ATM transaction, payment, deposit or other credit listed on your statement. Be sure that your register shows any interest paid into your account and any service charges, automatic payments or ATM transactions withdrawn from your account during this statement period.<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
                <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Use the chart to the right to list any deposits, transfers to your account, outstanding checks, ATM withdrawals, ATM payments or any other withdrawals (including any from previous months) which are listed in your register but not shown on your statement.<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
            };
        }
</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-methods-addinstuctionaboutenter-addinstuctionaboutadd-addinstuctionaboutsubtract" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-methods-addinstuctionaboutenter-addinstuctionaboutadd-addinstuctionaboutsubtract"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The methods: AddInstuctionAboutENTER, AddInstuctionAboutADD, AddInstuctionAboutSUBTRACT</h6>
<p>The methods add the the "<strong>Instructions</strong>" block. See Fig. 17.</p>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/b6298d280abbf9ec2d745eed4de253cc15e2473580a7bc55159b61a0f6ab0aca/687474703a2f2f7372762d646576302e67656874736f66742e636f6d3a383038302f504446466c6f772f496d616765732f42616e6b4163636f756e7453746174656d656e744c617374576f726b7368656574496e737472742e706e67"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/b6298d280abbf9ec2d745eed4de253cc15e2473580a7bc55159b61a0f6ab0aca/687474703a2f2f7372762d646576302e67656874736f66742e636f6d3a383038302f504446466c6f772f496d616765732f42616e6b4163636f756e7453746174656d656e744c617374576f726b7368656574496e737472742e706e67" alt="Fig. 17" title="Instructions" data-canonical-src="http://srv-dev0.gehtsoft.com:8080/PDFFlow/Images/BankAccountStatementLastWorksheetInstrt.png" style="max-width:100%;"></a> Fig. 17</p>
<p>The figure is divided by brown horizontal lines into the parts added by each method.</p>
<p>These parts are the same type, but with different and complex content. The fact that the parts are the same type is reflected by the code methods that are almost the same.
Each method:</p>
<ul>
<li>Adds the title using the <strong>AddInstructionTitle</strong> method and passing it different margins above the title and different title texts;</li>
<li>Adds and sets the table with 2 columns, one column for the instructions and one column for the form with the input fields ($ ) using the <strong>ConfigureDescriptionFormTable</strong> method;</li>
<li>Fills the left column with the instructions using one of the following methods: the <strong>FillEndingBalanceENTER</strong>, the <strong>FillInstructionAnyDeposits</strong>, and the <strong>FillInstructionAnyWithdrawals</strong>;</li>
<li>Adds the form with the input fields using the following methods: the <strong>AddEndingBalanceForm</strong>, the <strong>AddAnyDepositsForm</strong>, and the <strong>AddAnyWithdrawalsForm</strong>.</li>
</ul>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-addinstructiontitle-method" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-addinstructiontitle-method"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The AddInstructionTitle method</h6>
<p>The method adds the paragraph with title using the <strong>Helper.AddParagraph</strong> method that takes the parameter of the <strong>Gehtsoft.PDFFlow.Builder.RepeatingAreaBuilder</strong> class.</p>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-configuredescriptionformtable-method" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-configuredescriptionformtable-method"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The ConfigureDescriptionFormTable method</h6>
<p>The method sets the table. The method adds 2 columns of the specified width and sets the margin to the table.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>        <span class="pl-k">private</span> <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">ConfigureDescriptionFormTable</span>(<span class="pl-en">TableBuilder</span> <span class="pl-smi">tableBuilder</span>, 
            <span class="pl-k">float</span> <span class="pl-smi">descriptionColumnPercent</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">64</span>, <span class="pl-k">float</span> <span class="pl-smi">formColumnPercent</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">36</span>)
        {
            <span class="pl-smi">tableBuilder</span>
                .<span class="pl-en">SetMarginTop</span>(<span class="pl-c1">1f</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">SetWidth</span>(<span class="pl-smi">XUnit</span>.<span class="pl-en">FromPercent</span>(<span class="pl-c1">100</span>))
                .<span class="pl-en">SetBorder</span>(<span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">None</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">SetAltRowStyleBackColor</span>(<span class="pl-smi">Color</span>.<span class="pl-smi">White</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">AddColumnPercentToTable</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-smi">descriptionColumnPercent</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">AddColumnPercentToTable</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-smi">formColumnPercent</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">SetAlignment</span>(<span class="pl-smi">HorizontalAlignment</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Left</span>);
        }
</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-methods-fillendingbalanceenter-fillinstructionanydeposits-fillinstructionanywithdrawals" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-methods-fillendingbalanceenter-fillinstructionanydeposits-fillinstructionanywithdrawals"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The methods: <strong>FillEndingBalanceENTER</strong>, <strong>FillInstructionAnyDeposits</strong>, <strong>FillInstructionAnyWithdrawals</strong></h6>
<p>The methods add the columns with instructions below the title of the instructions (the parts in Fig. 17 highlighted with brown rectangles)
Each method</p>
<ul>
<li>Creates the table for the item name and the instructions;</li>
<li>Sets the table equally using the <strong>ConfigureDescription</strong> method described above. The table consists of 2 columns.
Left narrow column is for item names: A, B, C, respectively. Right wide column is for instructions. This is done so that the text of the instructions are indented from the left margin by the width of the item name.</li>
<li>Adds items of the instructions using the <strong>AddDescriptionRow</strong> method for each item.
The item name, or space in case on no item name, and the action to add the item of the text instructions are passed to the method.  This is done using:
The <strong>AddDescriptionToCell</strong> method,
The <strong>AddCalculateDescriptionToCell</strong> method,
The <strong>AddWithdrawalsDescriptionToCell</strong> method,
The <strong>AddCalculateEndingBalanceDescriptionToCell</strong> method.</li>
</ul>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-adddescriptionrow-method" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-adddescriptionrow-method"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The AddDescriptionRow method</h6>
<p>The method</p>
<ul>
<li>Adds the row to the table;</li>
<li>Sets the minimum height of the row using the value passed in the parameter;</li>
<li>Fills the left cell of the row using the item name passed in the parameter;</li>
<li>Calls the action passed in the parameter for the right cell.</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>        <span class="pl-k">private</span> <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">AddDescriptionRow</span>(<span class="pl-en">TableBuilder</span> <span class="pl-smi">tableBuilder</span>, <span class="pl-k">float</span> <span class="pl-smi">minHeight</span>, 
            <span class="pl-k">string</span> <span class="pl-smi">listIndex</span>, <span class="pl-k">string</span>[] <span class="pl-smi">text</span>, 
            <span class="pl-en">Action</span>&lt;<span class="pl-en">TableCellBuilder</span>, <span class="pl-k">string</span>[]&gt; <span class="pl-smi">addTextAction</span>)
        {
            <span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-smi">rowBuilder</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">tableBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddRow</span>();
            <span class="pl-smi">rowBuilder</span>
                .<span class="pl-en">ApplyStyle</span>(
                    <span class="pl-smi">StyleBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">New</span>()
                        .<span class="pl-en">SetTableCellMinHeight</span>(<span class="pl-smi">minHeight</span>)
                );
            <span class="pl-smi">rowBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddCell</span>(<span class="pl-smi">listIndex</span>).<span class="pl-en">SetFont</span>(<span class="pl-smi">FNT7_2B</span>);
            <span class="pl-en">addTextAction</span>(<span class="pl-smi">rowBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddCell</span>(), <span class="pl-smi">text</span>);
        }
</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-adddescriptiontocell-method" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-adddescriptiontocell-method"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The AddDescriptionToCell method</h6>
<p>The method sets the cell specifying its font and dotted border.
The method adds the paragraphs for each string from the array passed in the parameter in the <strong>foreach</strong> cycle.
It is used by the methods:</p>
<ul>
<li>The <strong>FillEndingBalanceENTER</strong> to add the "<em>A</em>" item;</li>
<li>The <strong>FillInstructionAnyDeposits</strong>  to add the "<em>B</em>" item.</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>        <span class="pl-k">private</span> <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">AddDescriptionToCell</span>(<span class="pl-en">TableCellBuilder</span> <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>, <span class="pl-k">string</span>[] <span class="pl-smi">text</span>)
        {
            <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>
                .<span class="pl-en">SetFont</span>(<span class="pl-smi">FNT7_2</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">SetBorderStroke</span>(<span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">None</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">None</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">None</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Dotted</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">SetBorderColor</span>(<span class="pl-smi">Color</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Black</span>);
            <span class="pl-k">foreach</span> (<span class="pl-k">string</span> <span class="pl-smi">item</span> <span class="pl-k">in</span> <span class="pl-smi">text</span>)
            {
                <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddParagraphToCell</span>(<span class="pl-smi">item</span>);
            }
        }
</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-addcalculatedescriptiontocell-method" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-addcalculatedescriptiontocell-method"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The AddCalculateDescriptionToCell method</h6>
<p>The method sets the cell specifying its dotted border.
The method adds the paragraphs for each string from the array passed in the parameter in the <strong>for</strong> cycle.
The method sets the Bold font for the first paragraph.
It is used by the method:</p>
<ul>
<li>The <strong>FillInstructionAnyDeposits</strong> to add the "<em>CALCULATE THE SUBTOTAL</em>" item.</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>        <span class="pl-k">private</span> <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">AddCalculateDescriptionToCell</span>(<span class="pl-en">TableCellBuilder</span> <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>, 
            <span class="pl-k">string</span>[] <span class="pl-smi">text</span>)
        {
            <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>
                .<span class="pl-en">SetPadding</span>(<span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">10</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">SetBorderStroke</span>(<span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">None</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">None</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">None</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Dotted</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">SetBorderColor</span>(<span class="pl-smi">Color</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Black</span>);
            <span class="pl-k">for</span> (<span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-smi">i</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-smi">l</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">text</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Length</span>; <span class="pl-smi">i</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span> <span class="pl-smi">l</span>; <span class="pl-smi">i</span><span class="pl-k">++</span>)
            {
                <span class="pl-k">string</span> <span class="pl-smi">item</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">text</span>[<span class="pl-smi">i</span>];
                <span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-smi">font</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">i</span> <span class="pl-k">==</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span> <span class="pl-k">?</span> <span class="pl-smi">FNT7_2B</span> <span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-smi">FNT7_2</span>;
                <span class="pl-en">ParagraphBuilder</span> <span class="pl-smi">paragraphBuilder</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddParagraph</span>();
                <span class="pl-smi">paragraphBuilder</span>
                    .<span class="pl-en">SetFont</span>(<span class="pl-smi">font</span>)
                    .<span class="pl-en">AddText</span>(<span class="pl-smi">item</span>);
            }
        }
</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-addwithdrawalsdescriptiontocell-method" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-addwithdrawalsdescriptiontocell-method"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The AddWithdrawalsDescriptionToCell method</h6>
<p>The method sets the cell not to have any borders.
The method adds the paragraphs for each string from the array passed in the parameter in the <strong>foreach</strong> cycle.
It is used by the method:</p>
<ul>
<li>The <strong>FillInstructionAnyDeposits</strong> to add the "<em>C</em>" item.</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>        <span class="pl-k">private</span> <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">AddWithdrawalsDescriptionToCell</span>(<span class="pl-en">TableCellBuilder</span> <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>, 
            <span class="pl-k">string</span>[] <span class="pl-smi">text</span>)
        {
            <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>
                .<span class="pl-en">SetFont</span>(<span class="pl-smi">FNT7_2</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">SetBorderStroke</span>(<span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">None</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">None</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">None</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">None</span>);
            <span class="pl-k">foreach</span> (<span class="pl-k">string</span> <span class="pl-smi">item</span> <span class="pl-k">in</span> <span class="pl-smi">text</span>)
            {
                <span class="pl-en">ParagraphBuilder</span> <span class="pl-smi">paragraphBuilder</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddParagraph</span>();
                <span class="pl-smi">paragraphBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddText</span>(<span class="pl-smi">item</span>);
            }
        }
</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-addcalculateendingbalancedescriptiontocell-method" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-addcalculateendingbalancedescriptiontocell-method"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The AddCalculateEndingBalanceDescriptionToCell method</h6>
<p>The method sets the cell not to have any borders.
The method adds the paragraphs for each string from the array passed in the parameter in the <strong>for</strong> cycle.
The method sets the Bold font for the first paragraph.
It is used by the method:</p>
<ul>
<li>The <strong>FillInstructionAnyWithdrawals</strong> to add the "<em>CALCULATE THE ENDING BALANCE</em>" item.</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>        <span class="pl-k">private</span> <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">AddCalculateEndingBalanceDescriptionToCell</span>(
            <span class="pl-en">TableCellBuilder</span> <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>, <span class="pl-k">string</span>[] <span class="pl-smi">text</span>)
        {
            <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>
                .<span class="pl-en">SetPadding</span>(<span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">10</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">SetBorderStroke</span>(<span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">None</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">None</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">None</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">None</span>);
            <span class="pl-k">for</span> (<span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-smi">i</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-smi">l</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">text</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Length</span>; <span class="pl-smi">i</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span> <span class="pl-smi">l</span>; <span class="pl-smi">i</span><span class="pl-k">++</span>)
            {
                <span class="pl-k">string</span> <span class="pl-smi">item</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">text</span>[<span class="pl-smi">i</span>];
                <span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-smi">font</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">i</span> <span class="pl-k">==</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span> <span class="pl-k">?</span> <span class="pl-smi">FNT7_2B</span> <span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-smi">FNT7_2</span>;
                <span class="pl-en">ParagraphBuilder</span> <span class="pl-smi">paragraphBuilder</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddParagraph</span>();
                <span class="pl-smi">paragraphBuilder</span>
                    .<span class="pl-en">SetFont</span>(<span class="pl-smi">font</span>)
                    .<span class="pl-en">AddText</span>(<span class="pl-smi">item</span>);
            }
        }</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-methods-addendingbalanceform-addanydepositsform-addanywithdrawalsform" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-methods-addendingbalanceform-addanydepositsform-addanywithdrawalsform"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The methods: <strong>AddEndingBalanceForm</strong>, <strong>AddAnyDepositsForm</strong>, <strong>AddAnyWithdrawalsForm</strong></h6>
<p>The methods add the input forms in the "<strong>Instructions</strong>" block highlighted in Fig 18 with brown rectangles.</p>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/f725e446597d2814f791c109f32e5b78bed159b061b12225cea5c092008f604c/687474703a2f2f7372762d646576302e67656874736f66742e636f6d3a383038302f504446466c6f772f496d616765732f42616e6b4163636f756e7453746174656d656e744c617374576f726b7368656574466f726d732e706e67"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/f725e446597d2814f791c109f32e5b78bed159b061b12225cea5c092008f604c/687474703a2f2f7372762d646576302e67656874736f66742e636f6d3a383038302f504446466c6f772f496d616765732f42616e6b4163636f756e7453746174656d656e744c617374576f726b7368656574466f726d732e706e67" alt="Fig. 18" title="Forms" data-canonical-src="http://srv-dev0.gehtsoft.com:8080/PDFFlow/Images/BankAccountStatementLastWorksheetForms.png" style="max-width:100%;"></a> Fig. 18</p>
<p>The methods add different number of the form rows using the <strong>Helper.AddFormRow</strong>:</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>AddEndingBalanceForm</strong> - 1</li>
<li><strong>AddAnyDepositsForm</strong> - 6</li>
<li><strong>AddAnyWithdrawalsForm</strong> - 1</li>
</ul>
<p>The <strong>AddAnyWithdrawalsForm</strong> method adds the field in the rectangle to the second row form using the <strong>Helper.AddFormRowBox</strong> method.</p>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-addbalancecalc-method" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-addbalancecalc-method"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The AddBalanceCalc method</h6>
<p>The method adds the "<strong>Balance calculation</strong>" to the page. See Fig. 19.</p>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/107fe5767acc9c774719e6ac793866404e397f87238234ff66716f8695eb36d3/687474703a2f2f7372762d646576302e67656874736f66742e636f6d3a383038302f504446466c6f772f496d616765732f42616e6b4163636f756e7453746174656d656e744c61737443616c635461626c652e706e67"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/107fe5767acc9c774719e6ac793866404e397f87238234ff66716f8695eb36d3/687474703a2f2f7372762d646576302e67656874736f66742e636f6d3a383038302f504446466c6f772f496d616765732f42616e6b4163636f756e7453746174656d656e744c61737443616c635461626c652e706e67" alt="Fig. 19" title="Calculation" data-canonical-src="http://srv-dev0.gehtsoft.com:8080/PDFFlow/Images/BankAccountStatementLastCalcTable.png" style="max-width:100%;"></a> Fig. 19</p>
<p>This is the table with 3 columns. The method:</p>
<ul>
<li>Sets the borders for all rows;</li>
<li>Adds and sets the first row to make it without borders;</li>
<li>Fills the first row by headers;</li>
<li>Adds 26 empty row in the <strong>for</strong> cycle;</li>
<li>Adds and sets the last row to make it without borders;</li>
<li>Adds and sets the last row to make the cells of the row, except the last one, without borders;</li>
<li>Add the "<em>Total amount $</em>" text to the penultimate cell of the last row.</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>        <span class="pl-k">private</span> <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">AddBalanceCalc</span>(<span class="pl-en">RepeatingAreaBuilder</span> <span class="pl-smi">builder</span>)
        {
            <span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-smi">tableBuilder</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">builder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddTable</span>();
            <span class="pl-smi">tableBuilder</span>
                .<span class="pl-en">SetWidth</span>(<span class="pl-smi">XUnit</span>.<span class="pl-en">FromPercent</span>(<span class="pl-c1">90</span>))
                .<span class="pl-en">SetBorder</span>(<span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Solid</span>, <span class="pl-smi">Color</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Black</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0.5f</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">SetAltRowStyleBackColor</span>(<span class="pl-smi">Color</span>.<span class="pl-smi">White</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">AddColumnPercentToTable</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-c1">20</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">AddColumnPercentToTable</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-c1">60</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">AddColumnPercentToTable</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-c1">20</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">SetAlignment</span>(<span class="pl-smi">HorizontalAlignment</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Right</span>);
            <span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-smi">rowBuilder</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">tableBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddRow</span>();
            <span class="pl-k">foreach</span> (<span class="pl-k">string</span> <span class="pl-smi">head</span> <span class="pl-k">in</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-k">string</span>[] {
                                                    <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Number<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
                                                    <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Items Outstanding<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
                                                    <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Amount<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
                                                    })
            {
                <span class="pl-smi">rowBuilder</span>
                    .<span class="pl-en">AddCell</span>(<span class="pl-smi">head</span>).<span class="pl-en">ApplyStyle</span>(
                                <span class="pl-smi">StyleBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">New</span>()
                                    .<span class="pl-en">SetBorderStroke</span>(<span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">None</span>)
                                    .<span class="pl-en">SetFont</span>(<span class="pl-smi">FNT7B</span>)
                                    .<span class="pl-en">SetHorizontalAlignment</span>(
                                        <span class="pl-smi">HorizontalAlignment</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Center</span>)
                            );
            }
            <span class="pl-k">for</span>(<span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-smi">i</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>; <span class="pl-smi">i</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span> <span class="pl-c1">26</span>; <span class="pl-smi">i</span><span class="pl-k">++</span>)
            {
                <span class="pl-smi">rowBuilder</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">tableBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddRow</span>();
                <span class="pl-smi">rowBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddCellToRow</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>).<span class="pl-en">AddCellToRow</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>).<span class="pl-en">AddCellToRow</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);
            }
            <span class="pl-smi">rowBuilder</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">tableBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddRow</span>();
            <span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">rowBuilder</span>
                .<span class="pl-en">AddCell</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Total amount  $<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);
            <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>
                .<span class="pl-en">ApplyStyle</span>(
                    <span class="pl-smi">StyleBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">New</span>()
                        .<span class="pl-en">SetBorderStroke</span>(<span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">None</span>)
                        .<span class="pl-en">SetFont</span>(<span class="pl-smi">FNT7B</span>)
                        .<span class="pl-en">SetHorizontalAlignment</span>(
                            <span class="pl-smi">HorizontalAlignment</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Right</span>)
                        .<span class="pl-en">SetVerticalAlignment</span>(
                            <span class="pl-smi">VerticalAlignment</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Bottom</span>)
                )
                .<span class="pl-en">SetColSpan</span>(<span class="pl-c1">2</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">SetPadding</span>(<span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">4</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>);
            <span class="pl-smi">rowBuilder</span>
                .<span class="pl-en">AddCellToRow</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);
        }
</pre></div>
<h4><a id="user-content-9-the-helper-class" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#9-the-helper-class"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>9. The Helper class</h4>
<p>The static class was created in order to avoid a code duplication.</p>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-addparagraph-methods" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-addparagraph-methods"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The AddParagraph methods</h6>
<p>All methods add the text paragraphs to the containers passed to them in the same way.</p>
<p>The methods differ in the type of the first parameter.</p>
<p>The parameter can be:</p>
<ul>
<li>The <strong>cellBuilder</strong> - an object of the<strong>Gehtsoft.PDFFlow.Builder.TableCellBuilder</strong> class.</li>
<li>The <strong>sectionBuilder</strong> - an object of the <strong>Gehtsoft.PDFFlow.Builder.SectionBuilder</strong> class.</li>
<li>The <strong>builder</strong> - an object of the <strong>Gehtsoft.PDFFlow.Builder.RepeatingAreaBuilder</strong> class.</li>
</ul>
<p>In addition to the described above, the methods can have the following parameters:</p>
<ul>
<li>The <strong>topMagin</strong> - the optional parameter. float.  The margin value above the paragraph.</li>
<li>The <strong>text</strong> - the text of the paragraph.</li>
<li>The <strong>paragrpaphFont</strong> - the font of the text.</li>
<li>The <strong>bottomMagin</strong> - the optional parameter. float.  The margin value below the paragraph.</li>
</ul>
<p>The full list of the methods:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>        <span class="pl-k">public</span> <span class="pl-k">static</span> <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">AddParagraph</span>(<span class="pl-en">SectionBuilder</span> <span class="pl-smi">sectionBuilder</span>, <span class="pl-k">string</span> <span class="pl-smi">text</span>, 
                    <span class="pl-en">FontBuilder</span> <span class="pl-smi">paragrpaphFont</span>, <span class="pl-k">float</span> <span class="pl-smi">bottomMagin</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0.0f</span>)

        public static void AddParagraph(<span class="pl-en">SectionBuilder</span> <span class="pl-smi">sectionBuilder</span>, <span class="pl-k">float</span> <span class="pl-smi">topMagin</span>, 
            <span class="pl-k">string</span> <span class="pl-smi">text</span>, <span class="pl-en">FontBuilder</span> <span class="pl-smi">paragrpaphFont</span>, <span class="pl-k">float</span> <span class="pl-smi">bottomMagin</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0.0f</span>)

        public static void AddParagraph(<span class="pl-en">TableCellBuilder</span> <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>, <span class="pl-k">string</span> <span class="pl-smi">text</span>,
            <span class="pl-en">FontBuilder</span> <span class="pl-smi">paragrpaphFont</span>, <span class="pl-k">float</span> <span class="pl-smi">bottomMagin</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0.0f</span>)

        public static void AddParagraph(<span class="pl-en">TableCellBuilder</span> <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>, <span class="pl-k">float</span> <span class="pl-smi">topMagin</span>, 
            <span class="pl-k">string</span> <span class="pl-smi">text</span>,
            <span class="pl-en">FontBuilder</span> <span class="pl-smi">paragrpaphFont</span>, <span class="pl-k">float</span> <span class="pl-smi">bottomMagin</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0.0f</span>)

        public static void AddParagraph(<span class="pl-en">RepeatingAreaBuilder</span> <span class="pl-smi">builder</span>, <span class="pl-k">string</span> <span class="pl-smi">text</span>,
            <span class="pl-en">FontBuilder</span> <span class="pl-smi">paragrpaphFont</span>, <span class="pl-k">float</span> <span class="pl-smi">bottomMagin</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0.0f</span>)

        public static void AddParagraph(<span class="pl-en">RepeatingAreaBuilder</span> <span class="pl-smi">builder</span>, <span class="pl-k">float</span> <span class="pl-smi">topMagin</span>, 
            <span class="pl-k">string</span> <span class="pl-smi">text</span>,
            <span class="pl-en">FontBuilder</span> <span class="pl-smi">paragrpaphFont</span>, <span class="pl-k">float</span> <span class="pl-smi">bottomMagin</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0.0f</span>)</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-replacenulldate-method" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-replacenulldate-method"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The ReplaceNullDate method</h6>
<p>The method returns the date in text format in accordance with the passed format or a passed default value when null is passed instead of date.</p>
<p>The parameters:</p>
<ul>
<li>The <strong>date</strong> - the object of the DateTime class or null;</li>
<li>The <strong>format</strong> - the date display format, string;</li>
<li>The <strong>forNull</strong> - the returned value if null is passed in the <strong>date</strong> parameter.</li>
</ul>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-replacenullstr-method" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-replacenullstr-method"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The ReplaceNullStr method</h6>
<p>The method returns the passed string or a passed default value when null is passed instead of date.</p>
<p>The parameters:</p>
<ul>
<li>The <strong>value</strong> - the value that must be returned if it is not null, string;</li>
<li>The <strong>forNull</strong> - the returned value if null is passed in the <strong>value</strong> parameter.</li>
</ul>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-replacezerodouble-method" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-replacezerodouble-method"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The ReplaceZeroDouble method</h6>
<p>The method returns the text of the passed double value with the prefix or a passed default value without prefix if NaN or 0 is passed.</p>
<p>The parameters:</p>
<ul>
<li>The <strong>value</strong> - the value, double, to be converted to string;</li>
<li>The <strong>forZero</strong> - the returned value if NaN or 0 пis passed in the <strong>value</strong> parameter;</li>
<li>The <strong>currencyPrefix</strong> - optional prefix, default is an empty string.</li>
</ul>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-replacezeroint-method" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-replacezeroint-method"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The ReplaceZeroInt method</h6>
<p>The method returns the text of the passed int value or a passed default value if 0 is passed.</p>
<p>The parameters:</p>
<ul>
<li>The <strong>value</strong> - the value, int, to be converted to string;</li>
<li>The <strong>forZero</strong> - the returned value if 0 is passed in the <strong>value</strong> parameter.</li>
</ul>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-addformrow-method" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-addformrow-method"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The AddFormRow method</h6>
<p>The method adds the row in the text__________  form to the table's cell.</p>
<p>The parameters:</p>
<ul>
<li>The <strong>cellBuilder</strong> - theobject of the<strong>Gehtsoft.PDFFlow.Builder.TableCellBuilder</strong> class;</li>
<li>The <strong>text</strong> - the optional prefix, string, default is "$".</li>
</ul>
<p>The method uses <em>Tabulation</em> to form the underline.</p>
