<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>        <span class="pl-k">public</span> <span class="pl-k">static</span> <span class="pl-en">ParagraphBuilder</span> <span class="pl-en">AddFormRow</span>(<span class="pl-en">TableCellBuilder</span> <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>, 
            <span class="pl-k">string</span> <span class="pl-smi">text</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>$<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>)
        {
            <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddParagraph</span>()
                .<span class="pl-en">AddTabSymbol</span>()
                .<span class="pl-en">SetFont</span>(<span class="pl-smi">FNT7_2</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">AddTabulation</span>(<span class="pl-c1">30</span>, <span class="pl-smi">TabulationType</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Right</span>, <span class="pl-smi">TabulationLeading</span>.<span class="pl-smi">None</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">AddTextToParagraph</span>(<span class="pl-smi">text</span>, <span class="pl-smi">addTabulationSymbol</span>: <span class="pl-c1">true</span>)
                .<span class="pl-en">AddTabulation</span>(<span class="pl-c1">96</span>, <span class="pl-smi">TabulationType</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Right</span>, <span class="pl-smi">TabulationLeading</span>.<span class="pl-smi">BottomLine</span>);
        }
</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-addformrowbox-method" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-addformrowbox-method"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The AddFormRowBox method</h6>
<p>The method adds the row in the text__________ form to the table's cell placing the cell to the rectangle.</p>
<p>The parameters:</p>
<ul>
<li>The <strong>cellBuilder</strong> - An object of the<strong>Gehtsoft.PDFFlow.Builder.TableCellBuilder</strong> class;</li>
<li>The <strong>text</strong> - the optional prefix, string, default is "$".</li>
</ul>
<p>The method uses <em>Tabulation</em> to form the underline and the table form the rectangle.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>        <span class="pl-k">public</span> <span class="pl-k">static</span> <span class="pl-en">TableCellBuilder</span> <span class="pl-en">AddFormRowBox</span>(<span class="pl-en">TableCellBuilder</span> <span class="pl-smi">outerCellBuilder</span>, 
            <span class="pl-k">string</span> <span class="pl-smi">text</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>$<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>)
        {
            <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-smi">outerCellBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddTableToCell</span>(<span class="pl-smi">tableBuilder</span> <span class="pl-k">=&gt;</span> 
            {
                <span class="pl-smi">tableBuilder</span>
                    .<span class="pl-en">SetWidth</span>(<span class="pl-smi">XUnit</span>.<span class="pl-en">FromPercent</span>(<span class="pl-c1">76</span>))
                    .<span class="pl-en">SetContentRowStyleMinHeight</span>(<span class="pl-c1">25</span>)
                    .<span class="pl-en">SetAlignment</span>(<span class="pl-smi">HorizontalAlignment</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Right</span>)
                    .<span class="pl-en">AddColumnPercentToTable</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-c1">100</span>)
                    .<span class="pl-en">SetBorderStroke</span>(<span class="pl-smi">Stroke</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Solid</span>)
                    .<span class="pl-en">SetBorderColor</span>(<span class="pl-smi">Color</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Black</span>)
                    .<span class="pl-en">SetBorderWidth</span>(<span class="pl-c1">1.5f</span>);
                <span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">tableBuilder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddRow</span>().<span class="pl-en">SetMinHeight</span>(<span class="pl-c1">25</span>).<span class="pl-en">AddCell</span>();
                <span class="pl-smi">cellBuilder</span>
                    .<span class="pl-en">SetVerticalAlignment</span>(<span class="pl-smi">VerticalAlignment</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Bottom</span>)
                    .<span class="pl-en">SetPadding</span>(<span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">4</span>)
                    .<span class="pl-en">AddParagraph</span>()
                    .<span class="pl-en">AddTabSymbol</span>()
                    .<span class="pl-en">SetFont</span>(<span class="pl-smi">FNT7_2</span>)
                    .<span class="pl-en">AddTabulation</span>(<span class="pl-c1">6</span>, <span class="pl-smi">TabulationType</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Right</span>, <span class="pl-smi">TabulationLeading</span>.<span class="pl-smi">None</span>)
                    .<span class="pl-en">AddTextToParagraph</span>(<span class="pl-smi">text</span>, <span class="pl-smi">addTabulationSymbol</span>: <span class="pl-c1">true</span>)
                    .<span class="pl-en">AddTabulation</span>(<span class="pl-c1">72</span>, <span class="pl-smi">TabulationType</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Right</span>, <span class="pl-smi">TabulationLeading</span>.<span class="pl-smi">BottomLine</span>);
            });
        }</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-the-addnumberedlisttoparagraph-method" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-addnumberedlisttoparagraph-method"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The AddNumberedListToParagraph method</h6>
<p>The method adds the numbered list using the array of the strings passed to it in the <strong>items</strong> parameter.
The method adds the paragraph for each item of the array and sets the <strong>numbered</strong> type of the list item using the <strong>Gehtsoft.PDFFlow.Builder.ParagraphBuilder.SetListNumbered</strong> method.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cs"><pre>        <span class="pl-k">public</span> <span class="pl-k">static</span> <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">AddNumberedListToParagraph</span>(<span class="pl-en">RepeatingAreaBuilder</span> <span class="pl-smi">builder</span>, 
            <span class="pl-k">string</span>[] <span class="pl-smi">items</span>, <span class="pl-en">FontBuilder</span> <span class="pl-smi">font</span>, <span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-smi">leftMargin</span>)
        {
            <span class="pl-k">foreach</span> (<span class="pl-en">String</span> <span class="pl-smi">text</span> <span class="pl-k">in</span> <span class="pl-smi">items</span>)
            {
                <span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-smi">paragraphBuilder</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">builder</span>.<span class="pl-en">AddParagraph</span>();
                <span class="pl-smi">paragraphBuilder</span>
                    .<span class="pl-en">SetMarginLeft</span>(<span class="pl-smi">leftMargin</span>)
                    .<span class="pl-en">SetFont</span>(<span class="pl-smi">font</span>)
                    .<span class="pl-en">SetListNumbered</span>(<span class="pl-smi">NumerationStyle</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Arabic</span>)
                    .<span class="pl-en">AddTextToParagraph</span>(<span class="pl-smi">text</span>);
            }
        }
</pre></div>
</article>
  </div>
